# <a name="troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality-faqs"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-104">疑難排解 Windows Mixed Reality (常見問題) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-104">Troubleshooting Windows Mixed Reality (FAQs)</span></span>

## <a name="understanding-common-installation-error-messages"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-105">瞭解常見安裝錯誤訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-105">Understanding common installation error messages</span></span>

### <a name="your-pc-cant-run-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-106">「您的電腦無法執行 Windows Mixed Reality」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-106">"Your PC can’t run Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-107">您的電腦不符合執行 Windows Mixed Reality 所需的 [最低需求](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-107">Your PC doesn’t meet the [minimum requirements](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) needed to run Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-108">這可能是因為電腦的硬體安裝程式與 Windows Mixed Reality 不相容，或是因為您需要 [更新至最新版本的 Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-108">This could be because the computer’s hardware setup isn’t compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, or because you need to [update to the latest version of Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-109">請注意，Windows Mixed Reality 需要至少支援 WDDM 2.2 的圖形配接器驅動程式，因此請確定您已從製造商取得最新的驅動程式更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-109">Note that Windows Mixed Reality requires a graphics card driver that supports at least WDDM 2.2, so make sure you have the latest driver update from the manufacturer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-110">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 安裝程式指出您的圖形配接器不符合需求，而您認為它的確如此，請確定您的耳機已插入正確的卡片中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-110">If Windows Mixed Reality setup says your graphics card doesn’t meet the requirements and you think it does, make sure your headset is plugged into the correct card.</span></span>

### <a name="youre-nearly-therethis-pc-doesnt-meet-the-minimum-requirements-needed-to-run-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-111">「您差不多，這部電腦不符合執行 Windows Mixed Reality 所需的最低需求」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-111">"You’re nearly there—this PC doesn’t meet the minimum requirements needed to run Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-112">您的電腦不符合 Windows Mixed Reality 中最佳體驗所需的 [最低需求](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-112">Your PC doesn’t meet the [minimum requirements](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) needed for the best experience in Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-113">您的電腦可能可以執行沉浸式耳機，但可能無法執行某些應用程式，或可能發生效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-113">Your PC may be able to run an immersive headset, but may not be able to run certain applications or might have problems with performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-114">請注意，Windows Mixed Reality 需要至少支援 WDDM 2.2 的圖形配接器驅動程式，因此請確定您已從製造商取得最新的驅動程式更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-114">Note that Windows Mixed Reality requires a graphics card driver that supports at least WDDM 2.2, so make sure you have the latest driver update from the manufacturer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-115">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 安裝程式指出您的圖形配接器不符合需求，而您認為它的確如此，請確定您的耳機已插入正確的卡片中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-115">If Windows Mixed Reality setup says your graphics card doesn’t meet the requirements and you think it does, make sure your headset is plugged into the correct card.</span></span>

### <a name="before-we-can-set-up-windows-mixed-reality-your-administrator-will-need-to-enable-it-for-your-organization-learn-more"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-116">「在我們可以設定 Windows Mixed Reality 之前，您的系統管理員必須為您的組織啟用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-116">"Before we can set up Windows Mixed Reality, your administrator will need to enable it for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-117">深入瞭解」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-117">Learn More"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-118">您可能是在企業管理的網路上，而且您的組織使用 Windows Server Update Services (WSUS) 或有其他可能封鎖下載的原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-118">You are probably on an enterprise managed network and your organization is using Windows Server Update Services (WSUS) or has other policies that may block the download.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-119">請洽詢貴組織的 IT 部門或系統管理員，以 [啟用 Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/manage-windows-mixed-reality#enable)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-119">Contact your organization's IT department or system administrator to [enable Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/manage-windows-mixed-reality#enable).</span></span>

### <a name="we-couldnt-download-the-mixed-reality-software-or-hang-tight-while-we-do-some-downloading"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-120">「我們無法下載 mixed reality 軟體」或「在我們進行一些下載時無阻礙」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-120">"We couldn't download the mixed reality software" or "Hang tight while we do some downloading"</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-121">有時暫止的更新可能會封鎖混合的現實軟體下載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-121">Sometimes a pending update can block the Mixed Reality Software download.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-122">移至 [ **設定] > 更新 & 安全性 > Windows Update** 並確認 Windows Update 已開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-122">Go to **Settings > Update & security > Windows Update** and make sure Windows Update is turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-123">然後下載並安裝任何正在等待安裝的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-123">Then download and install any updates that are waiting to be installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-124">如果您在嘗試這些步驟時收到 Windows Update 的錯誤，請移至 [這裡](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-124">If you get an error with Windows Update when attempting these steps go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-125">請確定您的電腦已連線到網際網路，且至少有2GB 的可用儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-125">Make sure your PC is connected to the internet and has at least 2GB of free storage space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-126">檢查網路狀態： **設定 > 網路 & 網際網路 > 狀態** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-126">Check your network status at: **Settings > Network & Internet > Status** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-127">如果您無法連線到網際網路，請移至 [這裡](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10741/windows-10-fix-network-connection-issues) 以取得協助。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-127">If you are unable to connect to the internet go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10741/windows-10-fix-network-connection-issues) for help.</span></span>  
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-128">請重新開機您的電腦，然後再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-128">Restart your PC and try again.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-129">如果先前的解決方案無法運作，請嘗試：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-129">If the previous solutions don't work, try:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-130">如果您的 Wi-fi 網路連線設定為計量付費，請將它變更為「未 [計費](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/17452/windows-metered-internet-connections-faq)」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-130">If your Wi-Fi network connection is set to [metered](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/17452/windows-metered-internet-connections-faq), change it to unmetered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-131">若要關閉計量付費連線，請移至：設定 **> 網路 & 網際網路 > 狀態 > 變更連接屬性 > 設定為計量付費連線** ，然後選取 [關閉]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-131">To turn off a metered connection, go to: **Settings > Network & Internet > Status > Change connection properties > Set as metered connection** and select "Off".</span></span>  
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-132">如果您最近安裝了更新，可能會造成問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-132">If you recently installed an update, it can cause problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-133">我們不建議您移除任何已安裝的更新，尤其是安全性更新，以確保電腦的安全，但有時移除最新的更新可協助判斷問題的根源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-133">We don’t recommend that you remove any installed updates, especially security updates which keep your PC safe, but sometimes removing the most recent update can help determine the source of the problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-134">若要這樣做：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-134">To do this:</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-135">移至 [ **設定] > 更新 & 安全性 > 查看已安裝的更新歷程記錄 > 卸載更新**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-135">Go to **Settings > Update & Security > View Installed Update History > Uninstall Updates**</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-136">選取上次安裝的更新，然後選取 [卸載]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-136">Select the last update installed and "Uninstall".</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-137">當系統提示「您確定要卸載此更新嗎？」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-137">When prompted "Are you sure you want to uninstall this update?"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-138">回答「是」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-138">answer "Yes".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-139">如果您在嘗試這些步驟時收到錯誤，請移至 [這裡](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-139">If you get an error when attempting these steps go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors).</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-140">請重新開機您的電腦，然後再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-140">Restart your PC and try again.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-141">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 正確安裝，請在 [設定] > 下重新安裝最新的更新， **Windows Update > 檢查是否有更新** ，並查看 Windows Mixed Reality 是否持續運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-141">If Windows Mixed Reality installs correctly, reinstall the latest updates under **Settings > Windows Update > Check for Updates** and see if Windows Mixed Reality continues to work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-142">如果未正確安裝，請重新安裝最新的更新，並聯絡 Windows 支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-142">If it does not install correctly, reinstall the latest updates and contact Windows Support.</span></span> 

### <a name="something-went-wrong-and-we-couldnt-start-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-143">「發生問題，無法開始 Windows Mixed Reality」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-143">"Something went wrong, and we couldn't start Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-144">從電腦拔下耳機的兩條纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-144">Unplug both cables of your headset from the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-145">將電腦重新開機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-145">Restart the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-146">移至 [ **設定] > 更新 & 安全性 > Windows Update** 並確認已開啟 [Windows Update]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-146">Go to **Settings > Update & security > Windows Update** and make sure that Windows Update is turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-147">然後下載並安裝任何等候中的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-147">Then download and install any waiting updates.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-148">將您的耳機重新連接到電腦，然後再次嘗試安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-148">Reconnect your headset to the PC and then try setup again.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-149">如果上述步驟沒有作用，請嘗試卸載，然後重新安裝 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-149">If the above steps don’t work, try uninstalling and then reinstalling Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-150">移至 [ **設定 > 混合現實 > 卸載** ]，然後選取 [卸載]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-150">Go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Uninstall** and select "Uninstall".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-151">重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-151">Restart your PC.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-152">若要再次啟動安裝程式，只需將您的耳機插入您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-152">To start the setup process again, just plug your headset into your PC.</span></span>
    

## <a name="troubleshooting-setup-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-153">針對設定問題進行疑難排解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-153">Troubleshooting setup questions</span></span> 

### <a name="my-xbox-controller-isnt-working-with-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-154">我的 Xbox 控制器無法使用 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-154">My Xbox controller isn't working with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-155">確定您的控制器已開啟、完全收費，並連接到電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-155">Make sure your controller is turned on, fully charged, and connected to the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-156">更換控制器的電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-156">Replace the controller’s batteries.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-157">如果您使用 Bluetooth 控制器，請移至電腦上的 [ **設定] > 裝置 > 藍牙 &** 電腦上的其他裝置，並確定它已配對 (應該列在頁面) 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-157">If you're using a Bluetooth controller, go to **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** on your PC and make sure it's paired (it should be listed on the page).</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-direct-input-controllers-gamepad-mousekeyboard-into-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-158">我無法直接將輸入 (控制器、遊戲台、滑鼠/鍵盤) 到 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-158">I can't direct input (controllers, gamepad, mouse/keyboard) into Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-159">當您放入耳機時，輸入應該會透過耳機的狀態感應器自動切換至您的混合現實體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-159">When you put on your headset, input should automatically get toggled to your mixed reality experience through your headset's presence sensor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-160">您的桌面上應該會出現藍色橫條：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-160">A blue bar should appear on your Desktop:</span></span>

![將輸入導向耳機的 Windows Desktop](images/1050px-windowsy.png)

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-162">如果未自動切換輸入，您必須手動將輸入切換到耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-162">If input doesn't get toggled automatically, you will need to manually toggle input to your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-163">若要這麼做，您可以在鍵盤上輸入 **Windows 鍵 + Y** (以及將輸入切換回桌面) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-163">You can do this by typing **Windows Key + Y** on your keyboard (and the same to toggle input back to the desktop).</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-plug-in-my-headset-nothing-happens-the-mixed-reality-portal-doesnt-open"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-164">當我插入耳機時，不會發生任何事。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-164">When I plug in my headset, nothing happens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-165">混合實境入口不會開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-165">The Mixed Reality Portal doesn’t open.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-166">混合實境入口，會將您帶到 Windows Mixed Reality 安裝程式的應用程式，設計為在插入相容的耳機時自動開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-166">Mixed Reality Portal, the app that takes you through Windows Mixed Reality setup, is designed to open automatically when you plug in a compatible headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-167">如果未開啟，請移至 [開始]，然後在 [搜尋] 方塊中輸入 "混合實境入口"，從該處開啟應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-167">If it doesn’t open, go to Start and type "Mixed Reality Portal" in the Search box to open the app from there.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-168">如果找不到混合實境入口，這可能表示您需要 [更新至最新版本的 Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-168">If you can’t find Mixed Reality Portal, that might mean you need to [update to the latest version of Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq).</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-choose-between-seated-and-standing-and-all-experiences"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-169">如何? 在「站上和站內」和「所有體驗」之間做選擇？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-169">How do I choose between "Seated and standing" and "All experiences"?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-170">如果您在耳機設定或更新版本中選擇「已待命」，則會使用沒有界限的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-170">If you choose "Seated and standing", either during headset setup or later on, you'll be using your headset without a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-171">您可以離開或保持在同一處，但是您將不會有任何界限可協助您避免實體障礙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-171">You can sit down or stand up, but you'll otherwise need to stay in one place, as you’ll have no boundary to help you avoid physical obstacles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-172">某些應用程式可能是設計來搭配界限使用，因此您可能無法使用它們，或者如果您在沒有界限的情況下使用，則可能不會有相同的體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-172">Some apps might be designed to work with a boundary, so you might not be able to use them or you might not have the same experience if you use them without a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-173">請參閱「什麼是界限，為什麼應該建立一個？」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-173">See "What's a boundary and why should I create one?"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-174">以下是詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-174">below for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-175">如果您選擇 [所有體驗]，您將會設定界限，而且可以使用適用于界限的應用程式和體驗，以及不需要的應用程式和體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-175">If you choose "All experiences", you'll set up a boundary and you can use apps and experiences that work with a boundary as well as those that don't require one.</span></span> 

### <a name="learn-mixed-reality-didnt-run-on-first-launch-and-i-went-right-into-the-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-176">學習混合實境不會在第一次啟動時執行，而是直接進入 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-176">Learn Mixed Reality didn't run on first launch, and I went right into the Windows Mixed Reality home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-177">您可以遵循 [重新執行的步驟](learn-mixed-reality.md#how-do-i-re-run-the-learning-experience)，重新執行學習體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-177">You can re-run the learning experience by following the [re-run steps](learn-mixed-reality.md#how-do-i-re-run-the-learning-experience).</span></span> 


## <a name="boundary-setup-and-other-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-178">界限設定和其他問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-178">Boundary setup and other questions</span></span>

### <a name="whats-a-boundary-and-why-should-i-create-one"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-179">什麼是界限，以及為什麼應該建立一個界限？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-179">What's a boundary and why should I create one?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-180">界限會定義您在戴 Windows Mixed Reality 沉浸式耳機時，可以四處移動的區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-180">A boundary defines the area in which you can move around while you're wearing your Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-181">因為您在使用耳機時看不到您的周圍，所以請務必建立界限來協助避免阻礙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-181">Because you can't see your surroundings while you're using your headset, it's important to create a boundary to help you avoid obstacles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-182">界限在混合現實內部看起來像白色外框，當您接近它時，它就會出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-182">The boundary looks like a white outline inside mixed reality and appears when you come close to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-183">當您看到它時，會使您的移動變慢，並避免跨越界限或將樹幹延伸至外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-183">When you see it, slow your movements, and avoid crossing the boundary or extending your limbs beyond it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-184">界限內的區域應該是「傢俱」、「低燈燈燈」、「天花板風扇」等等，因此您不會在任何地方進行任何動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-184">The area inside the boundary should be free of furniture, low-hanging light fixtures, ceiling fans, etc. so you won't bump into or trip over anything.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-185">[瞭解 Windows Mixed Reality 中的健康狀態和安全性](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-185">[Learn about health and safety in Windows Mixed Reality](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort).</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-create-a-boundary"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-186">如何? 建立界限？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-186">How do I create a boundary?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-187">當您第一次設定耳機時，安裝應用程式 (混合實境入口) 將會引導您完成建立界限的步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-187">When you first set up your headset, the setup app (Mixed Reality Portal) will take you through the steps to create a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-188">但是您隨時都可以建立一個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-188">But you can create one at any time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-189">若要這樣做：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-189">To do this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-190">選取您桌面上的 [ **開始] > 混合實境入口** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-190">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** on your desktop.</span></span> 
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-191">開啟 [功能表]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-191">Open "Menu".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-192">選取 [執行安裝程式] 以建立新的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-192">Select "Run setup" to create a new boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-193">如果有其他人使用您的耳機，請務必瞭解界限，以及其使用方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-193">If someone else uses your headset, make sure they understand the boundary and how to use it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-194">如果您將耳機移至新位置，則必須設定適用于該空間的新界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-194">If you move your headset to a new location, you'll need to set up a new boundary that works for that space.</span></span>

### <a name="i-get-an-error-message-when-i-try-to-create-a-boundary"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-195">當我嘗試建立界限時，收到錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-195">I get an error message when I try to create a boundary.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-196">建立界限時，請勿太接近牆或其他障礙物。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-196">Don't get too close to a wall or other obstruction when creating a boundary.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-197">請務必將您的耳機保持在 waist 高度，並在追蹤界限時面對您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-197">Make sure to hold your headset at waist height, and face your computer while you trace the boundary.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-198">請確定感應器未遭到封鎖，且有足夠的光線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-198">Make sure the sensor isn’t blocked and there’s enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-199">您要追蹤的空間應大於三個正方形計量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-199">The space you’re tracing should be larger than three square meters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-200">空間不應太大或太複雜。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-200">The space should not be too large or too complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-201">不需要太多訣竅，就能繼續使用簡單的幾何形狀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-201">Stick to a simple geometric shape without a lot of twists and turns.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-202">當您進行追蹤時，請勿交叉回復自己的路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-202">Don’t cross back over your own path as you’re tracing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-203">如果您卡在角落，請從頭開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-203">If you get stuck in a corner, start over.</span></span>

### <a name="during-start-up-of-mixed-reality-im-stuck-at-the-step-turn-your-head-side-to-side-and-then-at-the-floor"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-204">在混合現實的啟動過程中，我會停滯在「將您的前端移至側面，然後在地面」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-204">During start up of Mixed Reality, I'm stuck at the step "Turn your head side to side, and then at the floor".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-205">此步驟可讓您的耳機辨識您的空間，並還原任何現有的虛擬樓層和界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-205">This step lets your headset recognize your space and restore any existing virtual floor and boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-206">當您放入耳機時，此掃描程式最多可能需要10秒鐘的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-206">When you put on your headset, this scanning process can take up to 10 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-207">完成之後，您將會在混合現實首頁中，否則系統會提示您再次設定界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-207">After it is complete, you will either be in the Mixed Reality Home or you will be prompted to set up your boundary again.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-208">如果掃描程式所花費的時間超過10秒，則耳機中的鄰近感應器可能會發生問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-208">If the scanning process takes longer than 10 seconds, there could be a problem with the proximity sensor in the headset:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-209">檢查是否已從鄰近感應器移除不乾膠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-209">Check that the sticker has been removed from the proximity sensor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-210">近接感應器位於耳機內，大約是您冷汗中心的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-210">The proximity sensor is located inside the headset roughly where the center of your forehead would be.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-211">檢查您的鄰近感應器是否正在將輸入切換至您的耳機：使用手指，在確認輸入正在切換到耳機時，請先涵蓋並找出鄰近感應器數次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-211">Check that your proximity sensor is toggling input to your headset: with your finger, cover and uncover the proximity sensor a few times to verify input is switching to the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-212">您應該會在電腦頂端看到 **Windows 鍵 + Y** 橫幅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-212">You should see the **Windows Key + Y** banner at the top of your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-213">您可以在鍵盤上輸入 **Windows 鍵 + Y** ，隨時手動將輸入切換到耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-213">You can manually switch input to the headset at any time by typing **Windows Key + Y** on your keyboard.</span></span>

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-my-boundary-cant-be-found-what-should-i-do"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-214">我看到一則訊息，指出找不到我的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-214">I see a message that says my boundary can't be found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-215">我該怎麼辦？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-215">What should I do?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-216">Windows Mixed Reality 可能無法識別您的現有界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-216">Windows Mixed Reality might have trouble identifying your existing boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-217">您可以建立新的界限，也可以在「站上和站上」模式中使用您的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-217">You can create a new boundary or you can use your device in "Seated and standing" mode.</span></span> 

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-lost-tracking-or-we-dont-have-a-boundary-for-this-space"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-218">我看到一則訊息，指出「遺失追蹤」或「我們沒有這個空間的界限」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-218">I see a message that says “Lost tracking” or “We don’t have a boundary for this space”.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-219">您必須建立新的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-219">You must create a new boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-220">若要這樣做：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-220">To do this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-221">選取 [ **開始] > 混合實境入口** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-221">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-222">選取 [執行安裝程式]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-222">Select "Run setup".</span></span>

### <a name="the-boundary-is-always-visible-how-can-i-make-it-go-away"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-223">界限一律可見。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-223">The boundary is always visible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-224">如何讓它消失？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-224">How can I make it go away?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-225">當您接近界限時，即會顯示界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-225">The boundary appears when you are close to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-226">如果您的界限包含任何具有窄或不規則圖形的區段，您最後可能會接近它，並使其出現，比您想要的還多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-226">If your boundary includes any sections that have a narrow or irregular shape, you might end up getting close to it, and causing it to appear, more often than you’d like.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-227">若要修正此問題，請嘗試使用較大且更一般的圖形再次建立您的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-227">To fix this, try creating your boundary again using a larger and more regular shape.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-228">若要這樣做：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-228">To do this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-229">選取 [ **開始] > 混合實境入口** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-229">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-230">選取 [執行安裝程式]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-230">Select "Run setup".</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-turn-off-the-boundary-temporarily"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-231">如何暫時關閉界限？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-231">How can I turn off the boundary temporarily?</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-232">選取 [ **開始] > 混合實境入口** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-232">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-233">開啟 [功能表]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-233">Open "Menu".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-234">將「界限」變成「關閉」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-234">Turn "Boundary" to "Off".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-235">當界限關閉時，請務必保持在一個位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-235">Make sure to stay in one place while the boundary is off.</span></span>


## <a name="problems-in-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-236">Windows Mixed Reality 首頁的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-236">Problems in Windows Mixed Reality Home</span></span>

### <a name="my-controllers-arent-showing-in-my-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-237">我的控制器不會顯示在我的 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-237">My controllers aren't showing in my Windows Mixed Reality Home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-238">請確定您的控制器具有完整的電池，且已使用藍牙正確配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-238">Make sure your controllers have full batteries and that they are paired correctly using Bluetooth.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-239">請嘗試使用 Windows 按鈕關閉和開啟控制器電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-239">Try powering the controllers off and on using the Windows Button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-240">如果您仍然看不到您的控制器，請在 [ **裝置] > 藍牙** ] 下的 [設定] 功能表中，嘗試配對並重新配對各控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-240">If you still cannot see your controllers, try in-pairing and re-pairing each controller in the Settings menu under **Devices > Bluetooth** .</span></span>

### <a name="the-floor-of-my-windows-mixed-reality-home-doesnt-appear-to-be-at-the-correct-height-or-it-is-slanted"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-241">我的 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁的樓層似乎不是正確的高度，也不是傾斜的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-241">The floor of my Windows Mixed Reality Home doesn't appear to be at the correct height, or it is slanted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-242">選取 [ **開始] > 房間調整** ，一旦您將應用程式放在世界中，就會啟動，以在佩戴耳機時進行變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-242">Select **Start > Room Adjustment** which will launch once you place the app in the world, to make changes while wearing your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-243">在此應用程式中，系統會將您導向使用觸控板 (移動控制器) 或方向 (板) 來調整樓層高度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-243">In this app, you will be directed to use the touch pad (motion controller) or direction pad (gamepad) to adjust the floor height.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-244">當地面感覺正確時，請使用 Windows 按鈕來結束您的首頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-244">When the floor feels correct, use the Windows button to exit back to your Home.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-has-stopped-tracking"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-245">我的耳機已停止追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-245">My headset has stopped tracking.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-246">請確定燈開啟，而且沒有任何阻礙在耳機前方的內部追蹤攝影機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-246">Make sure the lights are on and that there isn't anything obstructing the inside-out tracking cameras on the front of your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-247">如果遺失追蹤，可能需要幾秒鐘的時間才能繼續。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-247">If tracking is lost, it can take a few seconds to resume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-248">如果追蹤未繼續，請嘗試重新開機 Windows Mixed Reality 入口網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-248">If tracking does not resume, try restarting the Windows Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-249">如需詳細資料，請參閱 [追蹤疑難排解](tracking.md) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-249">See [Tracking Troubleshooting](tracking.md) for more details.</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-show-a-preview-of-what-im-seeing-in-my-headset-on-my-desktop-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-250">我無法在我的桌上型電腦螢幕上，顯示我在耳機中看到的預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-250">I can't show a preview of what I'm seeing in my headset on my desktop screen.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-251">混合實境入口在畫面底部有一個 [ **播放** ] 按鈕，可讓您在桌面畫面上顯示您在耳機中看到的內容預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-251">Mixed Reality Portal has a **Play** button at the bottom of the screen that allows you to show a preview of what you're seeing in your headset on your desktop's screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-252">但基於效能考慮，只有在 Windows Mixed Reality Ultra (90Hz) 的電腦上才能使用此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-252">But for performance reasons, this feature is only available on PCs running at Windows Mixed Reality Ultra (90Hz).</span></span>

## <a name="headset-connectivity-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-253">耳機連接問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-253">Headset connectivity issues</span></span>

### <a name="my-computer-does-not-have-an-hdmi-port"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-254">我的電腦沒有 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-254">My computer does not have an HDMI port.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-255">如果您的電腦沒有 HDMI 埠，但是有 DisplayPort (DP) 、迷你 DisplayPort (miniDP) 或 USB 類型 C (USB C) 埠來輸出影片，您可能需要使用 [支援的介面卡](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-255">If your computer does not have an HDMI port but does have a DisplayPort (DP), mini DisplayPort (miniDP) or USB Type-C (USB-C) port for outputting video, you may need to use a [supported adapter](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md).</span></span>

### <a name="can-i-use-usb-or-hdmi-extension-cables-with-windows-mixed-reality-headsets"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-256">我可以使用 USB 或 HDMI 擴充纜線搭配 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-256">Can I use USB or HDMI extension cables with Windows Mixed Reality headsets?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-257">Windows Mixed Reality 耳機未正式支援使用 USB 或 HDMI 延伸模組纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-257">Windows Mixed Reality headsets do not officially support the use of USB or HDMI extension cables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-258">使用這些纜線可能會大幅影響您的混合現實體驗，原因是您電腦的 USB 控制器與混合現實耳機之間的信號完整性與匯流排電源之間的差異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-258">Using these cables may significantly impact your Mixed Reality experience because of variances in resulting signal integrity and bus power between your PC's USB controller and the Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-259">如果耳機顯示器短暫顯示藍色畫面，然後在使用時開啟黑色和混合實境入口重新開機或完全解除列舉，或是當耳機音訊剪出或變成 glitchy，或是當耳機在黑色和正確顯示器之間閃爍時，請嘗試使用沒有分機線的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-259">If the headset display briefly shows a blue screen and then turn black and Mixed Reality Portal restarts or completely de-enumerates during use, or if the headset audio cuts out or becomes glitchy, or if the headset flickers between black and the correct display, try using your headset without extension cables.</span></span>

### <a name="i-am-getting-a-check-your-display-cable-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-260">我收到「檢查您的顯示器纜線」錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-260">I am getting a "Check your display cable" error.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-261">如果您使用任何介面卡將耳機連接到您的電腦，請確定其支援 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-261">If you are using any adapters to connect your headset to your PC, make sure they support Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-262">此外，請先嘗試將介面卡連線到電腦，再將 HMD 連接至介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-262">Also try connecting the adapter to the PC before connecting the HMD to the adapter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-263">如果您的電腦同時具有整合式和離散圖形，請確定您使用的是使用中的圖形配接器上的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-263">If your PC has both integrated and discrete graphics, make sure you're using the HDMI port on your active graphics card.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-264">在某些情況下，這可能表示您必須將您的電腦顯示器連接至非 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-264">In some cases, this may mean that you'll need to connect your PC display to a non HDMI port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-265">如果您的電腦同時具有整合式和離散圖形，且整合式圖形較舊且不支援 Windows Mixed Reality，請嘗試停用整合式 GPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-265">If your PC has both integrated and discrete graphics, and the integrated graphics is older and does not support Windows Mixed Reality, try disabling the integrated GPU.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-266">將電腦監視器連接到電腦的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-266">Connect a PC monitor to your PC's HDMI port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-267">請確定您的圖形驅動程式是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-267">Make sure your graphics drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-268">直接從 AMD、Nvidia 或 Intel 下載並安裝，因為它們可能會比發行至 Windows Update 的版本還新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-268">Download and install the ones from AMD, Nvidia or Intel directly as they will likely be newer than what's published to Windows Update.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-269">請確定您已將耳機的 HDMI 纜線插入電腦上的 **hdmi 輸出** 埠，而不是埠中的 hdmi。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-269">Make sure that you plugged your headset's HDMI cable into an **HDMI out** port on your PC, not an HDMI in port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-270">Windows 可能無法偵測到顯示器纜線連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-270">Windows may be unable to detect the display cable connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-271">開啟裝置管理員，並查看耳機是否列在 [監視器] 之下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-271">Open the Device Manager and see if the headset is listed under "Monitors".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-272">如果沒有，請選取 [ **動作] > 掃描硬體變更** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-272">If not, select **Action > Scan for hardware changes** .</span></span> 

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-put-on-your-headset-even-though-i-have-my-headset-on"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-273">我看到一則訊息，指出「放在您的耳機」上，即使我有耳機也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-273">I see a message that says "Put on your headset" even though I have my headset on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-274">當您放入耳機時，Windows Mixed Reality 可能需要幾秒鐘的時間才能重載您的空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-274">When you put on your headset, Windows Mixed Reality may need a few seconds to reload your space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-275">如果這則訊息不會消失，請確定已從鄰近性感應器移除保護貼紙，其位於鏡頭之間的耳機內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-275">If this message doesn't go away, make sure the protective sticker has been removed from the proximity sensor, which is on the inside of the headset between the lenses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-276">如果這無法解決問題，請洽詢您的耳機製造商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-276">If this doesn't resolve the problem, contact your headset manufacturer.</span></span>

### <a name="a-message-says-connect-your-headset-even-though-ive-plugged-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-277">即使我已接上耳機，還是會顯示「連接您的耳機」訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-277">A message says "Connect your headset" even though I’ve plugged in my headset.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-278">請確定耳機的 USB 和 HDMI 纜線已連接到您電腦上的正確埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-278">Make sure the headset's USB and HDMI cables are connected to the correct ports on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-279">以下說明如何識別正確的埠：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-279">Here is how to identify the correct ports:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-280">USB 3.0 埠具有特殊標誌，其 "SS" 標示 (表示 "SuperSpeed" ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-280">USB 3.0 ports have a special logo with an "SS" mark (indicating "SuperSpeed").</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-281">埠的內部部分通常是藍色，而較舊的 USB 2.0 埠通常是在內部的黑色或白色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-281">The port's inside piece is normally blue, whereas older USB 2.0 ports are typically black or white on the inside.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-282">如果您的電腦有兩個 HDMI 埠，請使用連接到圖形配接器的埠，而不是電腦的主機板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-282">If your computer has two HDMI ports, use the one that connects to the graphics card, not the computer's motherboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-283">這並不一定很明顯，但離散埠通常位於電腦的展開位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-283">It's not always obvious which is which, though discrete ports are often located in an expansion slot on the computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-284">如果您嘗試一個埠但無法運作，請嘗試其他埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-284">If you try one port and it doesn't work, try the other.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-285">拔掉並插上耳機的 USB 和 HDMI 纜線，以確定它們已安全地連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-285">Unplug and plug in the USB and HDMI cables from your headset to make sure they are securely connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-286">插入 USB 纜線時，請不要在插入 USB 纜線期間暫停。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-286">When plugging in the USB cable, try not to pause during insertion of the USB cable.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-287">開啟裝置管理員並確認您的耳機列在 [混合式現實裝置] 下方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-287">Open Device Manager and confirm that your headset is listed under "Mixed Reality devices".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-288">按兩下 [混合現實裝置] 下的耳機，並確認裝置狀態指出「此裝置運作正常」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-288">Double click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices" and confirm that the device status indicates "This device is working properly".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-289">裝置管理員中所列裝置上的黃色驚嘆號表示連接到您電腦的裝置所回報的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-289">Yellow exclamation marks on devices listed in Device Manager indicate errors reported by the devices connected to your PC.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-290">如果在裝置管理員中以黃色驚嘆號列出「Hololens 感應器」，請按兩下裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-290">If "Hololens Sensors" is listed with a yellow exclamation mark in Device Manager, double click on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-291">如果您看到「 **代碼10：未安裝此裝置的驅動程式」。此裝置沒有相容的驅動程式** 」，請依照 [指示](headset-connectivity.md#the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset) 手動安裝耳機驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-291">If you see a **"Code 10: The drivers for this device are not installed. There are no compatible drivers for this device"** , follow the [instructions](headset-connectivity.md#the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset) to manually install the headset driver.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-292">如果您在電腦上使用多個混合現實耳機，並且在之前手動安裝混合現實耳機驅動程式，則在某些情況下，手動驅動程式更新可能只會套用到目前連線的耳機，而不會套用到您的其他耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-292">If you use multiple Mixed Reality headsets on your PC and have manually installed the Mixed Reality headset driver before, in some circumstances the manual driver update may only apply to the headset connected at the time and not to your other headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-293">在此情況下，您會看到「程式 **代碼31：此裝置無法正常運作，因為 Windows 無法載入此裝置所需的驅動程式。 (代碼 31) 。裝置管理員中已不再提供所要求的 ALPC 訊息** 」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-293">In this case, you'll see **"Code 31: This device is not working properly because Windows cannot load the drivers required for this device. (Code 31). The ALPC message requested is no longer available"** in Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-294">在裝置管理員中，以滑鼠右鍵按一下 [混合式現實裝置] 下的耳機，然後選取 [卸載裝置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-294">In Device Manager, right click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices", and select "Uninstall device".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-295">選取 [確定] 以確認並 replug 您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-295">Select "OK" to confirm and then unplug and replug your headset.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-296">如果您看到耳機的部分列舉 (一系列 USB 裝置列舉，但裝置管理員) 中的「混合現實耳機」沒有任何內容，請嘗試使用外部電源的 USB 3.0 中樞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-296">If you're seeing partial enumeration of the headset (a series of USB devices enumerate, but nothing under "Mixed Reality headsets" in Device Manager), try an externally powered USB 3.0 hub.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-297">移至耳機製造商的網站，並更新您耳機的驅動程式和固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-297">Go to the headset manufacturer’s website and update the drivers and firmware for your headset.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-298">將您的耳機連接至另一部電腦，然後開啟裝置管理員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-298">Connect your headset to another PC and open Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-299">即使該電腦與 Windows Mixed Reality 不完全相容，您仍可查看耳機是否列舉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-299">Even if that PC is not fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, you can check to see if your headset enumerates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-300">如果您的耳機未在多部電腦上列舉，則可能發生硬體問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-300">If your headset does not enumerate on multiple PCs, it could have a hardware issue.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-301">**適用于 Surface 使用者的附注：** 較舊版本的 Surface Dock 和 Surface Book USB Hub 固件更新軟體與混合現實耳機不相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-301">**Note for Surface users:** Earlier versions of the Surface Dock and Surface Book USB Hub firmware update software are incompatible with Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-302">如果您在 Surface PC 上收到「連接耳機」訊息，請查看裝置管理員中是否有任何裝置回報「程式 **代碼10：裝置無法啟動」錯誤** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-302">If you get a "Connect your headset" message on a Surface PC, check to see if any devices are reporting a **"Code 10: The device cannot start" error** in Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-303">如果是，請 [移除衝突的驅動程式](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4032123/kinect-sensor-is-not-recognized-on-a-surface-book)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-303">If so, [remove the conflicting driver](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4032123/kinect-sensor-is-not-recognized-on-a-surface-book).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-304">您應該只需要做一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-304">You should only need to do this once.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-305">**請注意 Windows 10 N 使用者：** 如果您的電腦執行 Windows 10 N，在插入您的混合現實耳機之後，裝置管理員會看到「 **代碼28：安裝類別不存在或無效」錯誤** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-305">**Note for Windows 10 N users:** If your PC is running Windows 10 N, you'll see a **"Code 28: The install class is not present or is invalid" error** in Device Manager after plugging in your Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-306">Windows Mixed Reality 不支援 Windows 10 的 N 版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-306">N-editions of Windows 10 are not supported by Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-307">如需詳細資訊，請遵循下列 [指示](troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality.md#im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-307">Follow these [instructions](troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality.md#im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager) for more information.</span></span>

### <a name="a-message-says-check-your-usb-cable-or-insufficient-usb-speed"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-308">訊息顯示「檢查 USB 纜線」或「USB 速度不足」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-308">A message says "Check your USB cable" or "Insufficient USB speed".</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-309">確定您是在電腦上使用支援的 USB 3.0 埠：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-309">Make sure that you're using a supported USB 3.0 port on your PC:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-310">請確定您的耳機 USB 纜線已插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-310">Make sure that your headset's USB cable is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-311">執行 [Windows Mixed Reality PC Check](https://aka.ms/pccheckapp) 應用程式，以確定您的電腦 USB 3.0 控制器受到支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-311">Run the [Windows Mixed Reality PC Check](https://aka.ms/pccheckapp) app to make sure your PC's USB 3.0 controller is supported.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-312">嘗試電腦上的每個其他 USB 3.0 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-312">Try each of the other USB 3.0 ports on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-313">有些電腦有一個以上的 USB 3.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-313">Some PCs have more than one USB 3.0 controller.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-314">暫時中斷連接到您電腦的所有 USB 裝置，並只連接您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-314">Temporarily disconnect all of the USB devices attached to your PC, and only connect your headset.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-315">在自訂的電腦上，即使埠可能標示為 USB 3.0 埠，它還是可能連接到 USB 2.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-315">On custom-built PCs, even though a port may be marked as a USB 3.0 port, it may be connected to a USB 2.0 controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-316">在您的耳機連接後，開啟裝置管理員，找出並按一下任何從您的耳機列舉的裝置，然後移至 [ **依連接查看 > 裝置** ]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-316">With your headset connected, open Device Manager, locate and single click any of the devices enumerated from your headset, then go to **View > Devices by connection** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-317">試用另一台電腦上的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-317">Try your headset on another PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-318">如果其他電腦與 Windows Mixed Reality 不完全相容，請簽入裝置管理員以查看是否看到「USB 速度不足」訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-318">If that other PC is not fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, check in Device Manager to see if you see the "insufficient USB speed" message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-319">如果您的耳機未在多部電腦上正確列舉，則您的耳機可能會有問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-319">If your headset does not enumerate properly on multiple PCs, your headset could be defective.</span></span>

### <a name="the-mixed-reality-portal-did-not-launch-automatically-after-i-plugged-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-320">插入耳機之後，混合實境入口並未自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-320">The Mixed Reality Portal did not launch automatically after I plugged in my headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-321">因為基礎問題，可能未正確偵測到耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-321">The headset might not have been detected properly because of an underlying issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-322">請嘗試手動啟動混合實境入口，並尋找出現的任何錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-322">Try launching the Mixed Reality Portal manually and look for any error messages that appear.</span></span> 

### <a name="my-headset-stopped-working-after-putting-my-pc-to-sleep-in-hibernation-mode-or-when-restarting-my-pc-with-my-headset-attached"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-323">我的耳機在讓電腦進入睡眠狀態、處於睡眠模式時，或在重新開機電腦時已連接我的耳機時，即停止運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-323">My headset stopped working after putting my PC to sleep, in hibernation mode, or when restarting my PC with my headset attached.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-324">開啟裝置管理員並確認您的耳機列在 [混合式現實裝置] 下方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-324">Open Device Manager and confirm that your headset is listed under "Mixed Reality devices".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-325">按兩下 [混合現實裝置] 下的耳機，並確認裝置狀態指出「此裝置運作正常」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-325">Double click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices" and confirm that the device status indicates "This device is working properly".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-326">如果您看到「代碼43」錯誤指出裝置已停止運作，或您沒有看到您的耳機列在「混合式現實裝置」底下，請在耳機的 USB 纜線中拔下並 replug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-326">If you see a "Code 43" error indicating that the device has stopped working, or if you don't see your headset listed under "Mixed Reality devices", unplug and replug in your headset's USB cable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-327">Microsoft 正在調查可能導致此錯誤的潛在軟體/驅動程式互通性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-327">Microsoft is investigating a potential software/driver interoperability issue which may result in this error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-328">此問題會影響少量的電腦，而且預期會在未來的混合現實耳機驅動程式更新中解決。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-328">This issue affects a small number of PCs, and is expected to be resolved in a future update to the Mixed Reality headset driver.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-causes-my-pc-to-generate-a-bug-check-blue-screen-when-i-put-my-pc-to-sleep-or-when-it-is-in-hibernation-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-329">當我讓電腦進入睡眠狀態或處於睡眠模式時，我的耳機會導致電腦產生錯誤檢查 (藍色螢幕) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-329">My headset causes my PC to generate a Bug Check (blue screen) when I put my PC to sleep or when it is in hibernation mode.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-330">Microsoft 正在調查可能的軟體/驅動程式互通性問題，這可能會導致少量的電腦產生「9F」錯誤檢查 (藍色畫面) 當電腦進入睡眠狀態或連接到耳機的睡眠模式時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-330">Microsoft is investigating a potential software/driver interoperability issue which may result in a small number of PCs potentially generating a "9F" Bug Check (blue screen) when the PC is put to sleep or into hibernation mode with the headset attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-331">這個問題預期會在未來的混合現實耳機驅動程式更新中解決。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-331">This issue is expected to be resolved in a future update to the Mixed Reality headset driver.</span></span>

### <a name="the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-332">當我插入耳機時，不會自動安裝耳機驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-332">The headset driver did not install automatically when I plugged in the headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-333">在新電腦上，或具有新安裝 Windows 10 複本的電腦上，耳機驅動程式可能會排在其他 Windows 更新後方，而且可能不會立即安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-333">On new PCs, or PCs with a newly installed copy of Windows 10, the headset driver could be queued behind other Windows updates and may not install immediately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-334">如果您有「N」個版本的 Windows，則必須切換至一般版本的 Windows 10，才能使用 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-334">If you have an "N"-edition of Windows, you will need to switch to a regular edition of Windows 10 to use Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-335">若要手動安裝：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-335">To install it manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-336">移至 [ **開始] > 裝置管理員** ，然後在 [其他裝置] 的 [hololens 感應器] 裝置中尋找黃色驚嘆號： ![ 裝置管理員 HoloLens 感應器的觀點](images/hololenssensors.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-336">Go to **Start > Device Manager** and look under "Other devices" for a "HoloLens Sensors" device with a yellow exclamation mark: ![View of Device Manager HoloLens Sensors](images/hololenssensors.png)</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-337">在裝置上按一下滑鼠右鍵，然後選取 [屬性]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-337">Right click on the device and select properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-338">如果裝置的 [內容] 讀取 **未安裝此裝置的驅動程式 (Code 28)** ，請關閉該視窗，然後繼續。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-338">If the device's properties read **The drivers for this device are not installed (Code 28)** , close the window and proceed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-339">如果有其他訊息，請遵循此頁面其餘部分的疑難排解步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-339">If there is another message, follow troubleshooting steps on the rest of this page.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-340">![裝置管理員中的 HoloLens 感應器的 Code 28](images/code28.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-340">![Code 28 of HoloLens Sensors in Device Manager](images/code28.png)</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-341">再以滑鼠右鍵按一下裝置，然後選取 [更新驅動程式 ...]然後，在裝置更新之後，[自動搜尋更新的驅動程式軟體]，您應該會在裝置管理員： ![ Mixed Reality 裝置出現在 [混合的現實裝置] 下方看到您的耳機：裝置管理員](images/mixedrealitydevices.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-341">Right click on the device again and select "Update Drivers..." and then "Search automatically for updated driver software" After the device updates, you should see your headset listed under "Mixed Reality devices" in Device Manager: ![Mixed Reality Device appear in Device Manager](images/mixedrealitydevices.png)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-342">如果手動安裝無法運作，或是您在其他裝置下找不到驅動程式，則您可能需要卸載現有的驅動程式並重新安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-342">If the manual install doesn’t work, or you don't find the driver under Other Devices, then you probably need to uninstall the existing driver and reinstall it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-343">若要這樣做：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-343">To do that:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-344">移至 [ **開始] > 裝置管理員** ，並查看耳機的 [混合的現實裝置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-344">Go to **Start > Device Manager** and look under "Mixed Reality devices" for your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-345">裝置狀態應該會指出「裝置運作正常」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-345">The device status should indicate that "The device is working properly".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-346">在裝置上按一下滑鼠右鍵，然後選取 [卸載裝置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-346">Right click on the device and select "Uninstall Device".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-347">在出現的新快顯視窗中，選取 [刪除此裝置的驅動程式軟體] 核取方塊，然後選取 [卸載]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-347">In the new popup that appears, select the check box "Delete the driver software for this device" and then select "Uninstall".</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-348">完成時，請從您的電腦拔下耳機，然後將它插回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-348">When that completes, unplug the headset from your PC, and plug it back in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-349">Windows Update 現在將會下載並安裝新的驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-349">Windows Update will now download and install a new driver.</span></span>

### <a name="troubleshooting-flowchart"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-350">疑難排解流程圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-350">Troubleshooting flowchart</span></span>

![連接您的耳機/檢查 USB 纜線](images/hmd-connectivity2.jpg)


## <a name="mixed-reality-headset-display-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-352">混合現實耳機顯示器問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-352">Mixed Reality headset display problems</span></span> ##

### <a name="my-headset-displays-are-black"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-353">我的耳機顯示器為黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-353">My headset displays are black.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-354">檢查您的電腦效能和穩定性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-354">Check your PC performance and stability:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-355">使用工作管理員查看是否有任何進程提高電腦的 CPU、GPU 及/或磁片磁碟機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-355">Use the Task Manager to see if any processes are maxing out your PC's CPU, GPU, and/or disk drives.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-356">使用事件檢視器) 查看 Windows (中的應用程式和系統事件記錄檔，以查看您的應用程式經常損毀，並產生 Windows 錯誤報告 (WER) 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-356">Look at the Applications and System Event Logs in Windows (using Event Viewer) to see if you have an app that is frequently crashing and generating Windows Error Reporting (WER) reports.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-357">請檢查 Windows Update，確定您的 Windows 版本是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-357">Check Windows Update to make sure your version of Windows is current.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-358">您可能必須選取 [檢查更新] 多次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-358">You may have to select "Check for Updates" multiple times.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-359">檢查應用程式和遊戲穩定性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-359">Check app and game stability:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-360">確定您的電腦符合最低系統需求，才能執行任何未正確執行的應用程式/遊戲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-360">Ensure that your PC meets the minimum system requirements to run any app/game that is not performing correctly.</span></span>    
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-361">確定您的 GPU 驅動程式版本是最新的，並檢查是否有新的效能和相容性問題，以及是否有新驅動程式的回歸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-361">Make sure your GPU driver version is recent, and check for any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on new drivers.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-362">如果您使用 SteamVR apps 和遊戲，請確定 SteamVR 和 SteamVR 元件的 Windows Mixed Reality 都是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-362">If you are using SteamVR apps and games, make sure SteamVR and the Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR components are up to date.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-363">檢查 HDMI 介面卡相容性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-363">Check HDMI adapter compatibility:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-364">請確定 HDMI 纜線已插入所有的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-364">Make sure that the HDMI cable is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-365">如果您使用的是 HDMI 介面卡 (例如，迷你 DisplayPort 至 HDMI 介面卡) ，請確定其與 Windows Mixed Reality 相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-365">If you're using an HDMI adapter (for example, a Mini DisplayPort to HDMI adapter), make sure it is compatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-366">介面卡必須支援 HDMI 2.0，而且有許多較舊的介面卡只支援1080p。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-366">The adapter must support HDMI 2.0, and there are many older adapters that only support 1080p.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-367">請參閱 [建議的 Windows Mixed Reality 配接器](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-367">See [Recommended adapters for Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs).</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-368">外掛程式可能很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-368">Plug order can be important.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-369">先將 HDMI 介面卡連線到您的電腦，再將耳機連接到介面卡，特別是當您使用的是 USB 至 HDMI 介面卡時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-369">Connect the HDMI adapter to your PC before connecting the headset to the adapter, especially if you're using a USB-C to HDMI adapter.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-370">如果您正在使用延伸模組纜線，請嘗試移除它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-370">Try removing extension cables if you are using them.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-371">檢查圖形配接器和驅動程式相容性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-371">Check graphics card and driver compatibility:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-372">使用電腦監視器來嘗試您電腦的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-372">Try your PC's HDMI port with a PC monitor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-373">有些電腦可能會有一個以上的 HDMI 埠，並非全部都在作用中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-373">Some PCs may have more than one HDMI port, and not all of them may be active.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-374">如果您的電腦同時具有整合式圖形處理器 (iGPU) 和離散圖形處理單元 (dGPU) ，請確定您已插入 dGPU 的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-374">If your PC has both an integrated graphics processing unit (iGPU) and a discrete graphics processing unit (dGPU), make sure that you are plugged into your dGPU's HDMI port.</span></span><br> ![HDMI 埠](images/HP_HDMI_Ports_s.png)
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-376">再次檢查您的 GPU 驅動程式版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-376">Double check your GPU driver version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-377">請確定它是最新的，但也請注意任何新的效能和相容性問題，以及對全新驅動程式的回歸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-377">Make sure it's recent, but also pay attention to any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on brand new drivers.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-378">如果您在膝上型電腦上使用 Mixed Reality，並且從圖形配接器製造商的網站安裝了較新的圖形驅動程式，請嘗試降級為電腦製造商網站或 Windows Update 上提供的最新圖形配接器驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-378">If you're using Mixed Reality on a laptop and you've installed a newer graphics driver from the graphics card manufacturer's website, try downgrading to the latest graphics card driver provided on your PC manufacturer's website, or on Windows Update.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-379">如果您有多部電腦監視器連接到您的電腦，請嘗試暫時中斷所有的電腦監視器，而不是一台電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-379">If you have multiple PC monitors connected to your PC, try temporarily disconnecting all but one PC monitor.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-380">如果您已為電腦監視器設定自訂的重新整理頻率，請嘗試暫時還原為標準的重新整理頻率，例如60Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-380">If you've set a custom refresh rate for your PC monitor, try temporarily reverting to a standard refresh rate, such as 60Hz.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-381">如果您最近變更了您的圖形配接器，但未重新安裝 Windows，請檢查耳機監視器是否仍安裝正確的驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-381">If you've recently changed your graphics card without reinstalling Windows, check that the headset monitor still has the correct driver installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-382">當您的耳機插入電源時，請確認裝置管理員中的 [監視] 節點底下已列出 [混合現實耳機]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-382">With your headset plugged in, confirm that "Mixed Reality headset" is listed under the Monitors node in Device Manager.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-383">如果您的電腦有 Nvidia 圖形卡，請確定 Nvidia 的3D 視覺軟體已停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-383">If your PC has an Nvidia graphics card, make sure that Nvidia's 3D Vision software is disabled.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-384">在某些圖形配接器上 (特別是較舊的圖形配接器) ，HDMI 埠可能不支援 HDMI 2.0，或可能無法完全與 Windows Mixed Reality 相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-384">On some graphics cards (especially older graphics cards), the HDMI port may not support HDMI 2.0 or may not be fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-385">請使用[主動 DisplayPort 1.2 至 HDMI 2.0 適配](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)卡來嘗試您的圖形配接器 DisplayPort 埠</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-385">Please try your graphics card's DisplayPort port by using an [active DisplayPort 1.2 to HDMI 2.0 adapter](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-386">Hp product number 1RJ99EA # 阿布達比的 HP Omen Pc 具有與 Windows Mixed Reality 不相容的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-386">HP Omen PCs with HP product number 1RJ99EA#ABU have HDMI ports that are incompatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-387">若要查看此情況，請開啟「HP 支援助理」，產品編號將會列在應用程式的底部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-387">To look this up, open up the "HP Support Assistant" and the product number will be listed towards the bottom of the app.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-388">如果您的電腦有 AMD Junos r 9 系列圖形介面卡，而您使用的是 Samsung Mixed Reality 耳機，您必須將耳機的固件更新為版本1.0.8 或更新版本，才能使用您的圖形配接器的 HDMI 埠搭配耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-388">If your PC has an AMD R9-series graphics card and you're using a Samsung Mixed Reality headset, you'll need to update your headset's firmware to version 1.0.8 or newer in order to use the HDMI port of your graphics card with the headset.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-389">如果您是使用 Surface Book 2，請確定您使用的是 [SURFACE USB-C 至 HDMI 介面卡](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-389">If you're using a Surface Book 2, please make sure you're using the [Surface USB-C to HDMI adapter](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-390">檢查是否有混合現實耳機硬體問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-390">Check for a Mixed Reality headset hardware issue:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-391">若要確認或排除混合現實耳機的硬體問題，請嘗試將您的混合現實耳機連接至另一台電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-391">To confirm or rule out hardware issues with your Mixed Reality headset, try connecting your Mixed Reality headset to another PC.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-392">請先檢查電腦相容性和安裝程式問題，因為徵兆很類似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-392">Check for PC compatibility and setup issues first, as the symptoms are very similar.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-393">請檢查以確定 USB 纜線已插入 USB 3.0 或更快的埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-393">Check to make sure the USB cable is plugged into a USB 3.0 or faster port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-394">USB 3.0 埠具有 SS () 在其旁邊寫入的速度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-394">USB 3.0 ports have SS (Super Speed) written next to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-395">它們通常 (，但不一定) 彩色藍色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-395">They are often (but not always) colored blue.</span></span>        

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-396">如果有説明，請參閱下列耳機黑色畫面疑難排解流程圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-396">If helpful, consult the headset black screen troubleshooting flow chart below.</span></span>
