### <a name="my-headset-display-occasionally-turns-black-after-some-use"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-398">在某些用途之後，我的耳機顯示器偶爾會變成黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-398">My headset display occasionally turns black after some use.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-399">請嘗試停用您電腦可能擁有的任何 USB 暫止或省電功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-399">Try disabling any USB suspend or power saving features your PC might have.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-400">例如，在 Windows 電源選項中， [USB 選擇性暫](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-selective-suspend) 止、在裝置管理員中將 [允許電腦關閉此裝置來節省電源] 設定，以及電腦上任何 USB 電源節約設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-400">For example, [USB selective suspend](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-selective-suspend) in Windows power options, the "Allow the computer to turn off this device to save power" setting in Device Manager, and any USB power saving settings in your PC's firmware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-401">暫時中斷連接到您電腦的任何其他 USB 裝置和週邊設備。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-401">Temporarily disconnect any other USB devices and peripherals connected to your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-402">再次檢查您的 GPU 驅動程式版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-402">Double check your GPU driver version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-403">請確定它是最新的，但也請注意任何新的效能和相容性問題，以及對全新驅動程式的回歸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-403">Make sure it's recent, but also pay attention to any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on brand new drivers.</span></span>

### <a name="one-of-the-displays-on-my-headset-is-black"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-404">耳機中的其中一個顯示為黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-404">One of the displays on my headset is black.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-405">如果您使用的是 HDMI 介面卡，請確定它支援 HDMI 2.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-405">If you're using an HDMI adapter, make sure it supports HDMI 2.0.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-406">移除任何您可能使用的 USB 和 HDMI 擴充纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-406">Remove any USB and HDMI extension cables that you may be using.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-407">請確定您的圖形驅動程式是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-407">Make sure your graphics driver is up-to-date.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-408">在另一部電腦上嘗試混合現實耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-408">Try the Mixed Reality headset on another PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-displays-turn-blue-for-a-moment-and-then-mixed-reality-portal-reinitializes"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-409">我的耳機會顯示一段時間的藍色，然後混合實境入口重新初始化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-409">My headset displays turn blue for a moment, and then Mixed Reality Portal reinitializes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-410">這通常表示您的電腦上發生偶爾的 USB 控制器可靠性問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-410">This typically indicates an occasional USB controller reliability issue on your PC:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-411">嘗試其他 USB 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-411">Try another USB port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-412">您的電腦可能有多個 USB 3.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-412">Your PC may have multiple USB 3.0 controllers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-413">如果適用)  (移除任何擴充纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-413">Remove any extension cables (if applicable).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-414">嘗試從您的電腦撥出所有其他 USB 裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-414">Try unplugging all other USB devices from your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-415">請嘗試將外部驅動的 USB 3.0 中樞連接到您的電腦，並將您的耳機連接至中樞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-415">Try connecting an externally-powered USB 3.0 hub to your PC, and connecting your headset to the hub.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-416">如果您使用的是桌上型電腦，請考慮購買 USB 3.0 PCIe 卡，以將另一個 USB 控制器新增至您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-416">If you're using a Desktop PC, consider purchasing a USB 3.0 PCIe card to add another USB controller to your PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-causes-my-pc-to-hang-or-show-a-black-screen-while-starting-up"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-417">我的耳機會導致電腦停止回應，或在啟動時顯示黑色畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-417">My headset causes my PC to hang or show a black screen while starting up.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-418">在某些電腦上，將您的耳機保持在開啟狀態，然後重新開機您的電腦，可能會干擾其啟動流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-418">On some PCs, leaving your headset plugged in before turning on or while rebooting your PC may interfere with its startup process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-419">您的電腦可以選取耳機顯示為「主要監視器」來顯示電腦的啟動進度，或無法正常啟動，而且可能會「停止回應」及/或產生嗶聲錯誤碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-419">Your PC could select the headset displays as the "primary monitor" to show PC startup progress or it could be prevented from starting up properly and may "hang" and/or produce a beeping error code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-420">此行為主要取決於 PC 製作和型號，以及/或圖形配接器的製作和型號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-420">The behavior depends largely on the PC make and model, and/or the make and model of the graphics card.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-421">修正方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-421">To fix this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-422">將您的耳機連接到您圖形配接器上的不同埠 (您可能需要使用介面卡來) 使用其他埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-422">Connect your headset to a different port on your graphics card (you may need to use an adapter to use the other ports).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-423">請確定電腦的 BIOS/UEFI 固件是最新的 (但如果您很熟悉) ，只會更新您電腦的 BIOS/UEFI 固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-423">Make sure your PC's BIOS / UEFI firmware is up-to-date (but only update your PC's BIOS / UEFI firmware if you're comfortable doing so).</span></span>

### <a name="my-pc-or-headset-displays-flicker-flash-or-remain-black-when-using-a-surface-pc"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-424">使用 Surface PC 時，我的電腦或耳機顯示器閃爍、閃爍或保持黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-424">My PC or headset displays flicker, flash or remain black when using a Surface PC.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-425">請確定您使用的是支援 HDMI 2.0 的 HDMI 介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-425">Make sure you're using an HDMI adapter that supports HDMI 2.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-426">許多較舊的 HDMI 介面卡僅支援1080p 解析度，這對混合現實耳機沒有足夠的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-426">Many older HDMI adapters only support 1080p resolution, which is insufficient for Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-427">請確定您的圖形驅動程式是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-427">Make sure your graphics driver is up-to-date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-428">除了檢查 Windows Update 之外，您可能還想要檢查電腦製造商的網站，以取得更新的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-428">In addition to checking Windows Update, you may wish to check the PC manufacturer's website for an updated graphics driver.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-429">某些表面裝置與 Windows Mixed Reality 不相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-429">Some Surface devices are incompatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-430">深入瞭解 [介面相容性和需求](windows-mixed-reality-minimum-pc-hardware-compatibility-guidelines.md#windows-mixed-reality-and-surface)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-430">Learn more about [Surface compatiblity and requirements](windows-mixed-reality-minimum-pc-hardware-compatibility-guidelines.md#windows-mixed-reality-and-surface).</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-display-doesnt-work-after-i-shut-down-and-do-a-fast-startup"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-431">當我關機並快速啟動時，我的耳機顯示器無法運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-431">My headset display doesn't work after I shut down and do a fast startup.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-432">從耳機拔下 HDMI 纜線和 USB 纜線，然後將其插回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-432">Unplug the HDMI cable and the USB cable from the headset and then plug them back in.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-displays-are-very-choppy-but-mixed-reality-portals-preview-window-appears-fine"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-433">我的耳機顯示器很穩定，但混合實境入口的預覽視窗看起來沒問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-433">My headset displays are very choppy, but Mixed Reality Portal's preview window appears fine.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-434">確定您的電腦系統資源 (的 CPU、記憶體和硬碟) 可供使用，而不是由另一個應用程式或進程進行限定或超量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-434">Make sure your PC's system resources (CPU, memory, and hard drive) are available and not pegged or maxed out by another app or process.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-435">更新您的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-435">Update your graphics driver.</span></span>

### <a name="im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-436">我收到裝置管理員中的「安裝類別不存在或無效」錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-436">I'm getting a "The install class is not present or is invalid" error in Device Manager.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-437">如果您在裝置管理員中看到有黃色驚嘆號的「HoloLens 感應器」，請按兩下裝置以取得其他詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-437">If you see "HoloLens Sensors" with a yellow exclamation mark in Device Manager, double click on the device for additional details.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-438">如果您看到一則訊息，指出「未安裝此裝置的驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-438">If you see a message saying "The drivers for this device are not installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-439"> (代碼 28) --安裝類別不存在或無效」，這通常是因為您的電腦正在 [Windows 10 N](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039813/media-feature-pack-for-windows-10-n-october-2017)執行。請注意，N 版的 Windows 10 不支援 Windows Mixed Reality，而且您必須安裝 Windows 10 的非 N 版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-439">(Code 28) -- The install class is not present or is invalid", this is typically because your PC is running [Windows 10 N](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039813/media-feature-pack-for-windows-10-n-october-2017). Please note that N-editions of Windows 10 do not support Windows Mixed Reality, and you'll need to install a non-N version of Windows 10.</span></span>

### <a name="my-wmr-environment-is-jittery-or-stutters-when-i-move-my-head-and-displays-double-vision"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-440">我的 WMR 環境會在移動前端並顯示雙重視覺時，抖動或口吃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-440">My WMR environment is jittery or stutters when I move my head and displays double vision.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-441">在具有整合式圖形和 Nvidia GPU 的膝上型電腦上，會在一段時間後發生錯誤，導致先前的畫面格在下一個畫面格之後顯示，導致雙重視覺效果加快偏擺、音調或變換移動頭部的速度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-441">On a laptop with integrated graphics and an Nvidia GPU, an error occurs after a period of time that appears to cause a previous frame to display after the next frame, resulting in double vision the faster you move your head in a yaw, pitch, or roll movement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-442">問題似乎是 Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48 之後的驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-442">The issue appears to be on drivers after Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="ba121-443">安裝此驅動程式將會修正此問題，直到 Nvidia 解決更新驅動程式中的問題為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-443">Installing this driver will fix the issue until Nvidia solves the problem in the updated drivers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-444">如需直接安裝 Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48，請造訪 [nvidia](https://www.nvidia.com/Download/driverResults.aspx/152007/en-us)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-444">For a direct install of Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48, visit [NVIDIA](https://www.nvidia.com/Download/driverResults.aspx/152007/en-us).</span></span>

### <a name="im-experiencing-discomfort-when-i-use-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-445">我在使用耳機時遇到不適感。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-445">I’m experiencing discomfort when I use my headset.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-446">如需在 Windows Mixed Reality 中緩和的一般資訊，請參閱 [Windows Mixed Reality 沉浸式耳機健康情況、安全和緩和](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-446">For general info about comfort in Windows Mixed Reality, see [Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset health, safety, and comfort](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-447">如需特定耳機的詳細資訊，請洽詢耳機製造商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-447">For details about your specific headset, check with the headset manufacturer.</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-get-a-clearer-view-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-448">我要如何在我的耳機中取得更清楚的觀點？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-448">How can I get a clearer view in my headset?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-449">請嘗試調整您耳機的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-449">Try adjusting the fit of your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-450">調整其在您臉部的位置，方法是將它向上或向下、向左和向右移動，然後調整母線使其感覺箱子。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-450">Adjust its position on your face by moving it up and down or left and right, and adjust the straps so it feels snug.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-451">如果您的耳機支援，您也可以調整其校正設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-451">If your headset supports it, you can also adjust its calibration settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-452">如果耳機有旋鈕來調整校正，請使用該旋鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-452">If the headset has a knob to adjust calibration, use that.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-453">如果不是，請移至 [ **設定] > Mixed reality > 視覺品質** ，並在該處調整校正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-453">If it doesn’t, go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Visual quality** and adjust the calibration there.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-454">如需有關特定裝置的校正的詳細資訊，請洽詢您的耳機製造商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-454">For more information on calibration for your specific device, check with your headset manufacturer.</span></span>

## <a name="mixed-reality-portal-error-messages-and-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-455">混合實境入口錯誤訊息和問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-455">Mixed Reality Portal error messages and problems</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-something-went-wrong-error-message-or-im-having-problems-in-the-mixed-reality-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-456">我收到「錯誤」的錯誤訊息，或混合實境入口發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-456">I got a "Something went wrong" error message, or I'm having problems in the Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-457">重新開機 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-457">Restart Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-458">從電腦中斷連接耳機纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-458">Disconnect both headset cables from your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-459">重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-459">Restart your PC.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-460">重新連接您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-460">Reconnect your headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-461">如果無法運作，請確定您的電腦能夠辨識您的耳機：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-461">If that doesn't work, make sure that your PC recognizes your headset:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-462">選取 [啟動]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-462">Select Start.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-463">在搜尋方塊中輸入「裝置管理員」，並在清單中選取它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-463">Type "device manager" in the search box and select it in the list.</span></span> 
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-464">展開 [混合現實裝置]，並查看是否已列出您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-464">Expand "Mixed reality devices" and see if your headset is listed.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-465">如果未列出，請嘗試下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-465">If it isn't listed, try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-466">將耳機插入電腦上的不同埠（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-466">Plug the headset into different ports on the PC, if available.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-467">從 Windows Update 檢查是否有最新的軟體更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-467">Check for the latest software updates from Windows Update.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-468">卸載並重新安裝 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-468">Uninstall and reinstall Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-469">從電腦中斷連接耳機纜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-469">Disconnect both headset cables from your PC.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-470">選取 [ **> 混合現實 > 卸載] 設定** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-470">Select **Settings  > Mixed reality > Uninstall** .</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-471">選取 **> 裝置 > 藍牙 & 其他裝置的設定** ，以將您的動作控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-471">Select **Settings  > Devices  > Bluetooth & other devices** to unpair your motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-472">選取每個控制器，然後選取 [移除裝置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-472">Select each controller, and then select "Remove device".</span></span>
    4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-473">將您的耳機插回電腦以重新安裝 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-473">Plug your headset back into your PC to reinstall Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>
    
### <a name="im-getting-a-check-your-usb-cable-error-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-474">我收到「檢查您的 USB 纜線」錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-474">I'm getting a "Check your USB cable" error message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-475">將您的耳機連接至不同的 USB 埠 (，並確定它是 SuperSpeed USB 3.0) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-475">Connect your headset to a different USB port (and make sure it’s a SuperSpeed USB 3.0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-476">此外，請嘗試移除耳機與電腦之間的任何擴充項或中樞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-476">Also, try removing any extenders or hubs between the headset and the computer.</span></span>

### <a name="im-getting-a-check-your-display-cable-error-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-477">我收到 [檢查您的顯示器纜線] 錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-477">I'm getting a "Check your display cable" error message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-478">嘗試下列作業：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-478">Try the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-479">將您的耳機連接至 DisplayPort 1.2 或更新版本，或 HDMI 1.4 或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-479">Connect your headset to a DisplayPort 1.2 or later, or HDMI 1.4 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-480">請確定埠與您電腦上最先進的圖形配接器相對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-480">Make sure the port corresponds with the most advanced graphics card on your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-481">如果您正在使用介面卡，請確定它可以使用4K。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-481">If you’re using an adapter, make sure it's 4K capable.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-482">請嘗試使用不同的 HDMI 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-482">Try using a different HDMI port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-483">如果您已將外部監視器插入至 HDMI 埠，請嘗試改為將其插入至 DisplayPort，並將 HDMI 埠用於耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-483">If you have an external monitor plugged into an HDMI port, try plugging it into a DisplayPort instead, and use the HDMI port for your headset.</span></span>

correctly.**</span></span> <br/><br/><ol start="1"><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-489">拔掉耳機的 USB 和 HDMI 纜線，然後將它們插回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-489">Unplug both your |   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-503">7-1、7-2、7-3/2181038087-1、2181038087-2、2181038087-3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-503">7-1, 7-2, 7-3  / 2181038087-1, 2181038087-2, 2181038087-3</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-504">**Windows Mixed Reality 連接到您的耳機時發生問題。請試著拔掉耳機，然後重新插入。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-504">**Windows Mixed Reality is having trouble connecting to your headset. |   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-508">7-4 / 2181038087-4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-508">7-4  / 2181038087-4</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-509">**Windows Mixed Reality 連接到您的耳機時發生問題。請試著拔掉耳機，然後重新插入。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-509">**Windows Mixed Reality is having trouble connecting to your headset. Try unplugging your headset and plugging it back in.**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="ba121-510">混合現實耳機驅動程式無法初始化您耳機上的追蹤攝影機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-510">The Mixed Reality headset driver failed to initialize the tracking cameras on your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-511">這很可能是暫時性錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-511">This is most likely a transient error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-512">拔掉您的耳機，然後重新插入，以解決此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-512">Unplug your headset and plug it in again to resolve this issue.</span></span>
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-513">7-5 / 2181038087-5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-513">7-5  / 2181038087-5</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-514">**Windows Mixed Reality 連接到您的耳機時發生問題。請嘗試將您的耳機插入不同的 USB 埠，並暫時拔掉連接到您電腦的任何其他 USB 裝置。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-514">**Windows Mixed Reality is having trouble connecting to your headset. Try plugging your headset into a different USB port and temporarily unplugging any other USB devices connected to your PC.**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="ba121-515">混合現實攝影機框架時間戳記與電腦時間戳記之間的 Windows Mixed Reality 遺失同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-515">Windows Mixed Reality lost synchronization between the Mixed Reality camera frame timestamps and your PC timestamps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-516">這可能是暫時性錯誤，或 USB 信號完整性問題的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-516">This could be a transient error, or an indication of USB signal integrity issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-517">修正方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-517">To fix this:</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-518">暫時拔掉所有 USB 裝置和週邊設備，移除所有的擴充纜線，然後只插入您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-518">Temporarily unplug all of your USB devices and peripherals, remove all extension cables, and plug in just your headset.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-519">在您的電腦上停用任何 USB 暫止/省電功能，例如在 Windows 電源選項中選擇 [暫停]、在裝置管理員中 [允許電腦關閉此裝置來節省電源] 設定，以及您電腦的固件中的任何 USB 省電設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-519">Disable any USB suspend/power saving features on your PC, like Selective suspend in Windows power options, the "Allow the computer to turn off this device to save power" setting in Device Manager, and any USB power saving settings in your PC's firmware.</span></span></li></ul>
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-520">7-6 / 2181038087-6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-520">7-6  / 2181038087-6</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-521">**耳機式固件發生問題。請試著拔掉耳機，然後重新插入。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-521">**There is a problem with your headset firmware. Try unplugging your headset and plugging it back in.**</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="ba121-522">這可能是暫時性錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-522">This can be transient error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-523">試著拔掉並重新插入耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-523">Try unplugging and re-plugging in your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-524">如果無法運作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-524">If that doesn't work:</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-525">檢查 Windows Update 以確定您執行的是最新的耳機驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-525">Check Windows Updates to ensure that you are running the latest headset driver available.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-526">試用另一台電腦上的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-526">Try your headset on another PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-527">如果您看到相同的錯誤訊息，則必須提供您的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-527">If you see the same error message, your headset will need to be serviced.</span></span></li></ul>

data-ttu-id="ba121-543">這些 USB 3.0 控制器驅動程式通常缺少讀取和處理 [ContainerID 描述](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-containerids-in-windows)項的能力，其會將混合現實耳機的不同部分匯總到同一個單元中， (從正確的耳機播放音訊、將正確的顯示器顯示出來，並從正確的感應器) 提取追蹤資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-543">These USB 3.0 controller drivers are often missing the ability to read and handle the (to play audio out of the correct headphones, video out the correct displays, and pull tracking data from the correct sensors).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-544">若要變更 USB 在名稱中沒有「Microsoft」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-546">Expand the category for Universal Serial Bus controllers and right click to uninstall the driver for each item that class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-547">Select "Delete the driver software for this device" to ensure the old drivers are removed.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-548">確認每個包含 "可延伸主機控制器" 文字的專案都在結尾有 "Microsoft"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-548">Verify that each item that includes the text "eXtensible Host Controller" has "Microsoft" at the end.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-549">插入 HMD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-549">Plug in the HMD.</span></span></li></ol><span data-ttu-id="ba121-550">或者，如果問題是間歇性的，HMD 可能無法正確地回應 HMD 驅動程式的命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-550">Alternatively, if the issue is intermittent, the HMD might not be properly responding to commands from the HMD driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-551">若要修正此問題，請將 HMD 插到30秒以上，然後將其插回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-551">To fix, unplug the the TrueColor capability, then try running Mixed Reality Portal again.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-590">在桌上型電腦上，從圖形配接器製造商的網站安裝最新的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-590">On a desktop PC, install the latest graphics driver from the graphics card manufacturer's website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-591">在膝上型電腦上，從膝上型電腦製造商的網站安裝適用于製造商和型號的最新圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-591">On a laptop, install the latest graphics driver for your make and model from the laptop manufacturer's website.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-592">如果您有協力廠商圖形或顯示軟體/附屬應用程式，請暫時卸載這些應用程式和驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-592">If you have third party graphics or display software/accessories, temporarily uninstall these apps and drivers.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-593">選取 [再試一次] 以查看是否為暫時性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-593">Select "Try again" to see if it's a transient issue.</span></span></li></ul> |
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-594">14-3/-</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-594">14-3  / -</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-595">**連接到您的耳機時發生問題。請嘗試移除您可能使用的任何擴充纜線，並確定您已將耳機連接到您的圖形配接器的正確埠。如果您使用的是任何介面卡，請確定它們與混合的現實都相容。如果您仍然遇到問題，請嘗試更新圖形驅動程式。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-595">**We ran into a problem connecting to your headset. Try removing any extension cables you might be using, and make sure you've connected the headset to the correct port for your graphics card. If you're using any adapters, make sure they're compatible with Mixed Reality. If you're still having problems, try updating your graphics driver.**</span></span> <br/><br/><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-596">如果您在電腦監視器上使用任何自訂模式或更新頻率，請嘗試將其重新整理率設定為60Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-596">If you're using any custom modes or refresh rates on your PC monitor, try setting their refresh rates to 60Hz.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-597">請確定您使用的任何介面卡支援 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-597">Make sure any adapters you are using support Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-598">請嘗試從圖形配接器製造商的網站安裝最新的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-598">Try installing the latest graphics driver from the graphics card manufacturer's website.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-599">按一下 [再試一次] 以查看是否為暫時性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-599">Click "Try again" to see if it's a transient issue.</span></span></li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-600">14-4/-</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-600">14-4  / -</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-601">**連接到您的耳機時發生問題。請嘗試移除您可能使用的任何擴充纜線，並確定您已將耳機連接到您的圖形配接器的正確埠。如果您使用的是任何介面卡，請確定它們與混合的現實都相容。如果您仍然遇到問題，請嘗試更新圖形驅動程式。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-601">**We ran into a problem connecting to your headset. Try removing any extension cables you might be using, and make sure you've connected the headset to the correct port for your graphics card. If you're using any adapters, make sure they're compatible with Mixed Reality. If you're still having problems, try updating your graphics driver.**</span></span> <br/><br/><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-602">電腦的電腦監視器可能比您的圖形配接器可支援的還要多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-602">Your PC may have more PC monitors connected than your graphics adapter can support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-603">將您的主要電腦監視器全部中斷連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-603">Disconnect all but your primary PC monitor.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-604">請確定您使用的任何介面卡支援 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-604">Make sure any adapters you are using support Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-605">從圖形配接器製造商的網站安裝最新的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-605">Install the latest graphics driver from the graphics card manufacturer's website.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-606">按一下 [再試一次] 以查看是否為暫時性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-606">Click "Try again" to see if it's a transient issue.</span></span></li></ul> |
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-607">15-5/-</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-607">15-5  / -</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-608">**混合實境入口已失去與核心混合現實及其相依的 Windows 元件的同步處理。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-608">**Mixed Reality Portal has lost synchronization with core Mixed Reality and Windows components it depends on.**</span></span><br/><br/><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-609">這可能是因為您的電腦發生效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-609">This could be caused by a performance issue with your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-610">請確定您的 CPU、GPU 和 HDD 未在工作管理員中限定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-610">Make sure your CPU, GPU and HDD are not pegged in Task Manager.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-611">暫時中斷所有其他 USB 裝置與電腦的連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-611">Temporarily disconnect all other USB devices from your PC.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-612">重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-612">Restart your PC.</span></span></li></ul> |
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-613">-/H0002000-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-613">-     / H0002000-0</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-614">**您電腦的作業系統進入不相符的狀態以進行 Windows Mixed Reality**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-614">**Your PC's operating system has gotten into a mismatched state for Windows Mixed Reality**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="ba121-615">檢查 Windows Update 是否有更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-615">Check Windows Updates for updates.</span></span> |
|   <span data-ttu-id="ba121-616">-/S0002261-101、S0002361-101</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-616">-     / S0002261-101, S0002361-101</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-617">**混合現實 shell 元件的問題，導致無法正確啟動混合實境入口**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-617">**A problem with a Mixed Reality shell component is preventing Mixed Reality Portal from starting properly**</span></span><br/><br/><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-618">在您的電腦上使用事件檢視器開啟應用程式記錄檔，以在您嘗試開始 Windows Mixed Reality 時，檢查是否有任何應用程式損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-618">Open the Application Log using Event Viewer on your PC to check for any application crashes at around the time you tried to start Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-619">請確定您的圖形驅動程式是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-619">Make sure your graphics driver is up-to-date.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-620">您使用的 HDMI 介面卡與 Windows Mixed Reality 不相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-620">The HDMI adapter you are using is incompatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-621">請參閱 [此處](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md)的支援和建議的 HDMI，以將 (DP 的迷你顯示器通訊埠) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-621">See the supported and recommended HDMI to mini display port (DP) dongle [here](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md).</span></span></li></ul> |


## <a name="motion-controller-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-622">移動控制器問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-622">Motion controller problems</span></span>

### <a name="my-motion-controllers-arent-working-properly"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-623">我的動作控制器無法正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-623">My Motion controllers aren't working properly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-624">如果您的 [動作控制器](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality) 沒有作用、未連線，或是當您戴耳機時看不到控制器的影像，請嘗試下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-624">If your [motion controllers](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality) aren’t working, aren't connecting, or if you don’t see an image of the controllers when you’re wearing your headset, try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-625">請確定您的控制器已開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-625">Make sure your controllers are turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-626">若要開啟它們，請按住 Windows 按鈕兩秒鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-626">To turn them on, press and hold the Windows button for two seconds.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-627">請確定控制器是完全收費的，如果不是，則更換電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-627">Make sure the controllers are fully charged and replace the batteries if they are not.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-628">將控制器放在您面前之前，請關閉並重新開啟控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-628">Turn the controllers off and on again while holding them in front of you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-629">按住 [Windows] 按鈕四秒鐘以關閉控制器，然後再按一次再按住兩秒鐘來開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-629">Press and hold the Windows button for four seconds to turn a controller off, then press and hold it again for two seconds to turn it on.</span></span> 
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-630">選取 [ **> 裝置的設定] > 藍牙 &** 電腦上的其他裝置，並確定控制器列示為配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-630">Select **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** on your PC and make sure the controllers are listed as paired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-631">如果不是，您必須將 [它們配對](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-631">If they’re not, you’ll need to [pair them](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality).</span></span> 
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-632">請確定移動控制器顯示為「已連線」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-632">Make sure the motion controllers show up as "Connected".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-633">「配對」不一定表示控制器會連接到電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-633">"Paired" does not necessarily mean the controllers are connected to the PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-634">控制器應該會出現在 [滑鼠、鍵盤 & 畫筆] 類別之下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-634">Controllers should appear under "Mouse, keyboard & pen" category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-635">[其他裝置] 下的移動控制器無法進行配對程式，且無法正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-635">Motion controllers under "Other devices" have failed the pairing process and are not functional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-636">檢查動作控制器 Led：已配對並連接明亮的控制器，dimly 亮控制器未連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-636">Check the motion controllers LEDs: Brightly lit controllers are paired and connected, dimly lit controllers aren't connected.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-637">移至 [ **開始] > 混合實境入口** 在您的電腦上，然後選取 [功能表]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-637">Go to **Start  > Mixed Reality Portal** on your PC and select "Menu".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-638">您應該會看到已列出您的動作控制器，以及狀態訊息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-638">You should see your motion controllers listed, along with a status message:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-639">就緒–控制器全都已設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-639">Ready – The controllers are all set.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-640">遺失追蹤–混合實境入口找不到您的控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-640">Lost tracking – Mixed Reality Portal can’t find your controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-641">將它們放在耳機前方，然後按下 [Windows] 按鈕4秒，再重新開機，再按2秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-641">Hold them in front of your headset and restart them by pressing the Windows button for 4 seconds, then again for 2 seconds.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-642">電力偏低–更換控制器電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-642">Low battery – Replace the controller batteries.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-643">如果您使用的是外部 USB 藍牙介面卡，請確定它已插入黑色 USB 2.0 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-643">If you're using an external USB Bluetooth Adapter, make sure it’s plugged into a black USB 2.0 port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-644">它也應該盡可能從任何其他無線發送器或 USB 快閃磁片磁碟機插入，包括耳機的 USB 連接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-644">It should also be plugged in as far away as possible from any other wireless transmitters or USB flash drives, including the USB connector for your headset.</span></span> 
8. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-645">在 Windows [開始] 功能表上按一下滑鼠右鍵，然後選取 [裝置管理員]，確認電腦上只有一個藍牙無線電。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-645">Verify that there’s only one Bluetooth radio in the PC by right clicking on the Windows Start Menu and select Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-646">展開 [藍牙] 區段，並尋找一個介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-646">Expand the Bluetooth section and look for one Adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-647">如果您使用具有內建無線電的桌上型電腦設定，請檢查是否已連接外部天線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-647">If you are using the desktop PC configuration with built-in radio, check if an external antenna is connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-648">如果沒有連線的外部天線，可能會導致追蹤問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-648">If there is no external antenna connected, it can cause tracking issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-649">或使用外部藍牙轉換器 (USB) 、停用內部藍牙功能，然後重試配對和連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-649">Or use an external bluetooth dongle (USB), disable the internal Bluetooth capability, and retry pairing and connecting.</span></span>
9. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-650">關閉 [藍牙設定] 視窗（如果已開啟）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-650">Close the Bluetooth settings window if it's open.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-651">如果是在背景中開啟，則會對藍牙通訊協定進行許多額外的呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-651">If it is open in the background, a lot of extra calls are made to the Bluetooth protocol.</span></span>
10. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-652">檢查移動控制器上的虛擬電池音量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-652">Check the virtual battery level on the motion controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-653">在 [混合式事實] 中，開啟控制器，您就可以看到電池圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-653">In mixed reality, turn the controllers over, and you'll be able to see a battery icon.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-654">若為紅色，則更換電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-654">If it is red, replace the batteries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-655">電池報告通常會在連接控制器後立即回報高於實際層級的報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-655">Battery reporting typically reports higher than the actual level immediately after connecting a controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-656">等候約15秒，讓電池計量穩定，然後閱讀層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-656">Wait about 15 seconds to let the battery level stabilize and then read the level.</span></span>
11. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-657">在 [設定] > 裝置中移除藍牙耳機和喇叭 **> 藍牙 & 其他裝置** ，然後關閉裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-657">Remove Bluetooth headphones and speakers in **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** , and turn the devices off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-658">在您的混合現實耳機上使用耳機插口或內建喇叭，以獲得最佳的音訊體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-658">Use the headphone jack or built-in speakers on your Mixed Reality headset for the best audio experience.</span></span>
12. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-659">如果您有其他 Bluetooth 裝置與您的電腦（例如耳機或 gamepads）配對，請將其移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-659">If you have other Bluetooth devices paired with your PC, such as headphones or gamepads, remove some of them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-660">選取 [ **> 裝置的設定] > 藍牙 & 電腦上的其他裝置** ，選取裝置，然後選取 [移除裝置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-660">Select **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices on your PC** , select the devices, and then select "Remove device".</span></span>
13. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-661">拔掉耳機上的 USB 纜線，然後將它插回電腦以重新開機電腦上的控制器功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-661">Unplug the USB cable on your headset and plugging it back into the PC to restart the controller functionality on the PC.</span></span>
14. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-662">控制器燈在進行固件更新時閃爍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-662">Controller lights flash when they are undergoing a firmware update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-663">等候固件更新完成，控制器應該會出現在混合的現實中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-663">Wait for the firmware update to complete and the controllers should appear in Mixed Reality.</span></span>
15. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-664">請確定您的電腦已連線到5GHz 的 Wi-fi 網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-664">Make sure your PC is connected to a 5GHz Wi-Fi network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-665">如果您的膝上型電腦連線到 2.4 GHz Wifi 網路，通常會共用藍牙連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-665">If your laptop is connected to a 2.4GHz Wifi network, it is typically sharing the Bluetooth connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-666">這可能會對 Wifi 或藍牙效能造成負面影響，視產品設計而定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-666">This may negatively impact either Wifi or Bluetooth performance, depending on the product design.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-667">在網路介面卡設定中，將慣用的頻外變更為5Ghz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-667">Change the preferred band to 5Ghz in the network adapter settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-668">如果您的網路不支援5GHz，則可以使用藍牙轉換器，而不是使用內部藍牙功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-668">If your network does not support 5GHz, a Bluetooth dongle can be used instead of the internal Bluetooth capability.</span></span>
16. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-669">如果您的藍牙設定已經配對，除非已將新的裝置移除，否則除非已使用特定的轉換器新增裝置，否則 Windows 將不會探索新裝置 (如果已使用特定的轉換器來新增裝置，則只能將其與該轉換器) 移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-669">If your Bluetooth settings have motion controllers already paired, Windows won’t discover the new devices until those are removed (if they have been added using a specific dongle, they can be only removed with that dongle).</span></span>
17. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-670">如果您的電腦有內建的藍牙，而您遇到連線問題，請嘗試改用 USB 藍牙介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-670">If your PC has built-in Bluetooth and you’re having connection problems, try using a USB Bluetooth adapter instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-671">若要這樣做，您必須關閉裝置管理員中的內建藍牙無線電，然後將其他 Bluetooth 裝置與新的介面卡配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-671">To do this, you’ll need to turn off your built-in Bluetooth radio in Device Manager and then pair your other Bluetooth devices with the new adapter.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controller-troubleshooting-flowchart"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-672">移動控制器疑難排解流程圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-672">Motion controller troubleshooting flowchart</span></span>

### <a name="my-controller-is-stuck-in-an-infinite-reboot-buzzing-after-leds-cycle"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-674">我的控制器卡在) 的 Led 迴圈之後，在無限重新開機 (聲止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-674">My controller is stuck in an infinite reboot (buzzing after LEDs cycle).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-675">這是很重要的電池指標，因此請確定您的裝置有新的電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-675">This is a critical battery indicator, so make sure you have fresh batteries in the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-676">如果問題持續發生，請執行 [裝置](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-restore-the-controllers-to-factory-settings) 復原，將控制器重設為原廠設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-676">If the issue persists, perform [device recovery](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-restore-the-controllers-to-factory-settings) to reset the controller to factory settings.</span></span>

### <a name="im-trying-to-pair-my-controllers-but-they-never-show-up-in-the-add-a-new-device-menu-in-bluetooth-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-677">我正在嘗試配對控制器，但它們永遠不會顯示在 [藍牙設定] 的 [新增裝置] 功能表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-677">I'm trying to pair my controllers, but they never show up in the "Add a new device menu" in Bluetooth Settings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-678">檢查您是否已有未配對的控制器，請將其移除，然後再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-678">Check that you do not have controllers paired already, remove them and try again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-679">如果問題持續發生，請重新開機電腦，然後再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-679">If problem persists restart the PC and try again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-680">如果失敗，請參閱 [藍牙常見問題](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-680">If that fails, consult the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span>

### <a name="wi-fi-speeds-becomes-slow-on-my-notebook-when-motion-controllers-are-turned-on"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-681">開啟運動控制器時，wi-fi 速度會變慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-681">Wi-Fi speeds becomes slow on my notebook when motion controllers are turned on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-682">連線至 2.4 GHz 存取點時，您的筆記本可以與藍牙共用其 Wi-fi 天線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-682">Your notebook may share its Wi-Fi antenna with Bluetooth when connected to 2.4GHz access point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-683">如果您可以將波段喜好設定切換為5GHz，請從 [裝置管理員] 進行檢查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-683">Check from device manager if you can switch band preference to 5GHz.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-684">如果無法使用5GHz 網路，而且效能受到嚴重的影響，請考慮使用藍牙轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-684">If 5GHz network is not available and performance is severely impacted, consider using a Bluetooth dongle.</span></span>

![您可以透過 [裝置管理員] 找到 Wifi 波段選項設定](images/wifi5ghz.png)

### <a name="my-second-controller-takes-a-long-time-to-reconnect"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-686">我的第二個控制器需要很長的時間才能重新連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-686">My second controller takes a long time to reconnect.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-687">當移動控制器同時開啟時，某些較舊的 Intel 無線電波會遇到此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-687">Some older Intel radios experience this issue if motion controllers are powered on at the same time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-688">避免同時開啟控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-688">Avoid powering on controllers at the same time.</span></span>

### <a name="my-qualcomm-bluetooth-radio-cannot-pair-controllers-after-a-pc-crash"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-689">我的 Qualcomm 藍牙無線電無法在電腦損毀之後配對控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-689">My Qualcomm Bluetooth radio cannot pair controllers after a PC crash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-690">Qualcomm (QCA) 之前的藍牙無線電驅動程式在 Windows 損毀之後可能會處於不良狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-690">Qualcomm (QCA) Bluetooth radio drivers prior to 10.0.0.448 may end up in bad state after a Windows crash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-691">完全關閉電腦的電源來解決這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-691">Power off the PC completely to workaround this problem.</span></span> 

### <a name="im-experiencing-poor-controller-tracking-with-marvell-radio"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-692">我在使用 Marvell 無線電時遇到不良的控制器追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-692">I'm experiencing poor controller tracking with Marvell radio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-693">移至 **裝置管理員 > 藍牙 > MARVELL AVASTAR 藍牙無線電介面卡 > 屬性 > 驅動程式** ，並確定您使用的是驅動程式15.68.9210.47 或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-693">Go to **Device Manager > Bluetooth > Marvell AVASTAR Bluetooth Radio Adapter > Properties > Driver** and make sure that you are using driver 15.68.9210.47 or later.</span></span>

### <a name="the-mixed-reality-portal-is-working-but-my-motion-controllers-are-tracking-poorly-controllers-keep-flying-away-shaking-etc"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-694">混合實境入口可正常運作，但我的運動控制器正在追蹤不佳 (控制器會保持飛出、搖動等 ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-694">The Mixed Reality Portal is working, but my motion controllers are tracking poorly (controllers keep flying away, shaking, etc.).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-695">某些照明條件可能會影響追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-695">Some lighting conditions can affect tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-696">請確定您不會暴露在直接照明的情況下，而且您的 (HMD 不會看到很多的點光源，例如，像是耶誕節樹狀結構的燈等字串) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-696">Make sure that you are not exposed to direct sunlight and that you don't have a lot of point light sources visible to your HMD (for example, strings of lights like a christmas tree).</span></span> 
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-697">查看 [藍牙常見問題](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-697">Check the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-698">這些徵兆通常是因為控制器與主機電腦之間的通訊失敗，並指出藍牙連結品質不佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-698">These symptoms are generally caused by failures to communicate between the controller and the host PC, and indicate poor Bluetooth link quality.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controller-leds-are-not-lit-but-the-buttons-and-thumbstick-still-work-in-mixed-reality-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-699">移動控制器 Led 不亮，但按鈕和操縱杆仍能在混合實境入口中運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-699">Motion Controller LEDs are not lit, but the buttons and thumbstick still work in Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-700">移動控制器校正快取可能已損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-700">The Motion Controller calibration cache may be corrupt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-701">若要刪除快取，請在系統管理員命令提示字元中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-701">To delete the cache, run the following command in an Administrator Command Prompt:</span></span>

`rmdir /S /Q C:\Windows\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\Windows\MotionController\Calibration`

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-702">此資料夾無法在 Windows 檔案總管中存取，而且只能從系統管理員命令提示字元修改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-702">This folder is not accessible in Windows Explorer and can only be modified from an Administrator Command Prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-703">刪除資料夾之後，請重新開機您的電腦，然後重新連接您的動作控制器來還原校正檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-703">After you have deleted the folder, restart your PC and reconnect your Motion Controllers to restore the calibration files.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controllers-do-not-appear-in-steamvr-apps-and-games"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-704">移動控制器不會出現在 SteamVR apps 和遊戲中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-704">Motion controllers do not appear in SteamVR apps and games.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-705">如果您能夠在 cliff 房子中看到您的運動控制器，但無法在 SteamVR 的應用程式和遊戲中看到，移動控制器模型驅動程式可能無法正確安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-705">If you're able to see your Motion Controllers in the cliff house, but not in SteamVR apps and games, the Motion Controller model driver may not be installed properly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-706">此驅動程式會透過 Windows Update 自動下載並安裝，但如果您是在具有企業原則的電腦上，或者如果 Windows Update 其他限制，您可能需要手動安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-706">This driver is automatically downloaded and installed via Windows Update, but if you're on a PC that has enterprise policies or if Windows Update is otherwise restricted, you may need to install this manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-707">若要檢查是否已正確安裝移動控制器模型驅動程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-707">To check that the Motion Controller model driver is correctly installed:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-708">開啟這兩個動作控制器，並確定它們在 [裝置] 下的 [設定] 應用程式中顯示為 [已連線]， **> 藍牙 & 其他裝置** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-708">Turn on both of your motion controllers, and make sure they show up as "Connected" in the Settings app under **Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-709">如果未顯示或顯示為「配對」，請將 [它們配對](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-709">If they do not show up or show up as "Paired", [pair them](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-710">開啟裝置管理員，然後在 [藍牙] 下尋找「移動控制器-左方」和「動作控制器-右側」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-710">Open Device Manager and look for "Motion controller - Left" and "Motion controller - Right" under "Bluetooth".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-711">選取 [裝置]，然後移至 [ **依連接查看 > 裝置** ]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-711">Select either device and then go to **View > Devices by Connection** .</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-712">您現在會看到移動控制器藍牙裝置匯總到藍牙無線電的觀看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-712">You will now see a view of the Motion Controller Bluetooth devices roll up to your Bluetooth radio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-713">在與兩個動作控制器相同的節點下，應該是兩個「Bluetooth HID 裝置」裝置，而且在每個藍牙 HID 裝置下都應該是名為「移動控制器」 (並) 灰色圖示的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-713">Under the same node as the two Motion Controllers should be two "Bluetooth HID Device" devices, and under each Bluetooth HID Device should be devices named "Motion Controller" (with gray icons).</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-714">按兩下每個「移動控制器」裝置，然後移至 [ **驅動程式** ] 索引標籤。確認列出的驅動程式版本對應到其中一個 [移動控制器模型驅動程式版本](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-714">Double click each of the "Motion Controller" devices and go to the **Driver** tab. Confirm that the Driver Version listed corresponds to one of [these Motion Controller model driver versions](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-715">若要手動下載並安裝移動控制器模型驅動程式，請流覽 [此頁面](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history) ，並尋找與您的 Windows 10 版本對應的驅動程式版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-715">To manually download and install the Motion Controller model driver, visit [this page](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history) and look for the driver version corresponding to your version of Windows 10.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-716">您可以從下載頁面取得安裝指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-716">Installation instructions are available on the download page.</span></span>

### <a name="the-motion-controllers-firmware-update-takes-significantly-longer-than-two-minutes"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-717">移動控制器固件更新花費的時間明顯超過兩分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-717">The Motion controllers firmware update takes significantly longer than two minutes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-718">查看 [藍牙常見問題](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-718">Check the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-719">藍牙連結品質不佳通常是這些問題的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-719">Poor Bluetooth link quality is usually the cause of these problems.</span></span>

### <a name="i-just-inserted-fresh-batteries-but-the-controller-virtual-battery-level-does-not-indicate-full-level"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-720">我剛剛插入了新電池，但是控制器的虛擬電池計量並沒有指出完整的層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-720">I just inserted fresh batteries but the controller virtual battery level does not indicate full level.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-721">移動控制器電池音量已針對 AA 電池調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-721">Motion controller battery level is tuned for AA batteries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-722">部分低電壓充電電池可能不會報告為完整，但會完全收費。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-722">Some low voltage rechargeable batteries may not report as full although being fully charged.</span></span>

### <a name="my-controller-does-not-vibrate-when-battery-is-low"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-723">當電池計量偏低時，我的控制器不會震動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-723">My controller does not vibrate when battery is low.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-724">當電池計量偏低時，會停用 Haptics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-724">Haptics is disabled when battery level gets low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-725">更換您的電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-725">Replace your batteries.</span></span>

### <a name="my-device-vibrated-three-times-and-then-shutdown"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-726">我的裝置 vibrated 三次，然後關機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-726">My device vibrated three times and then shutdown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-727">您的電池不足，並達到截止閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-727">Your batteries are running low and hit the cut-off threshold.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-728">更換您的電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-728">Replace your batteries.</span></span>

### <a name="my-samsung-motion-controllers-touchpad-is-off-center-or-has-a-dead-spot"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-729">我的 Samsung 移動控制器的觸控板已關閉，或有不正確位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-729">My Samsung motion controller’s touchpad is off-center or has a dead spot.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-730">這可能是硬體瑕疵，您應回到零售商或設備製造商，以進行更換或交換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-730">This is probably a hardware defect and you should go back to your retailer or equipment manufacturer for a replacement or exchange.</span></span>

### <a name="the-controller-isnt-working-correctly-and-i-cant-update-the-device"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-731">控制器無法正常運作，且無法更新裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-731">The controller isn't working correctly and I can't update the device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-732">將它還原至原廠條件 (您將需要全新的電池) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-732">Restore it to factory conditions (you will need fresh batteries):</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-733">拔掉控制器電源並關閉電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-733">Unplug and power off the controllers.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-734">開啟電池蓋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-734">Open the battery cover.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-735">插入新的電池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-735">Insert your new batteries.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-736">按住 [配對] 按鈕 (電池) 下底部的索引標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-736">Press and hold the pairing button (the tab at the bottom under the batteries).</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-737">按住 [配對] 按鈕時，按住 [Windows] 按鈕五秒，即可開啟控制器電源， (保持兩個按鈕) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-737">While holding the pairing button, power on the controller by pressing and holding the Windows button for five seconds (keep both buttons depressed).</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-738">釋放按鈕，並等候控制器開啟電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-738">Release the buttons and wait for controller to power on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-739">這最多需要15秒的時間，而且在裝置復原發生時不會有任何指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-739">This takes up to 15 seconds and there are no indicators when device recovery is happening.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-740">如果裝置在按鈕發行時立即開啟電源，修復按鈕序列就不會註冊，您必須再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-740">If device powers on immediately on button release, the recovery button sequence did not get registered and you need to try again.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-741">移至 [ **設定] > 藍牙 > 其他裝置** ]，然後選取 [移動控制器-左方] 或 [動作控制器-右方] 和 [移除裝置] ) 以從藍牙設定移除舊的控制器關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-741">Go to **Settings > Bluetooth > other devices** , and select "Motion controller - Left" or "Motion controller - Right" and "Remove device") to remove old controller associations from Bluetooth settings.</span></span> 
8. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-742">再次將控制器與電腦配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-742">Pair the controller with the PC again.</span></span>
9. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-743">連接主機和 HMD 之後，裝置將會更新至最新的可用固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-743">After connecting with the host and HMD, the device will update to the latest available firmware.</span></span>

### <a name="lights-and-indicators"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-744">燈光和指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-744">Lights and indicators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-745">LED constellation 環形和 haptics 指出移動控制器的狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-745">The LED constellation ring and haptics indicate the state of the motion controller.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-746">State</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-746">State</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-747">導致狀態的原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-747">What causes the state</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-748">與狀態相關聯的燈光和震動行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-748">Light and vibration behavior associated with the state</span></span> |
|----------------------------|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-749">**開啟電源**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-749">**Power on**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-750">按住控制器上的 Windows 按鈕兩秒，以開啟控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-750">Press and hold Windows button on controller for two seconds to turn on the controller.</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-751">Led 會開啟和控制器震動一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-751">LEDs turn on and controller vibrates once.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-752">**關閉電源**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-752">**Power off**</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-753">在控制器上按住 Windows 按鈕四秒鐘，以關閉控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-753">Press and hold Windows button on controller for four seconds to turn off controller.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-754">Led 關閉和控制器震動兩次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-754">LEDs turn off and controller vibrates twice.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-755">**休眠中**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-755">**Sleeping**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-756">當控制器 motionless 30 秒時，會自動進入睡眠狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-756">The controller enters sleeping state automatically when it’s motionless for 30 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-757">當控制器偵測到動作時，控制器會自動喚醒，但裝置未與主機電腦配對的情況除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-757">The controller automatically wakes when it detects motion except when the device is not paired with the host PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-758">在這種情況下，按下按鈕將需要喚醒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-758">In that case, a button press will be required to wake it up.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-759">Led 會在睡眠狀態下每三秒關閉並閃爍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-759">LEDs turn off and blink every three seconds while in sleeping state.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-760">**配對**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-760">**Pairing**</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-761">按下並按住電池內的配對按鈕三秒鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-761">Press and hold pairing button inside battery case for three seconds.</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-762">當配對模式時，Led 會慢慢地進入脈衝狀態，並在結束配對模式時進入穩固。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-762">LEDs slowly pulse while in pairing mode, and go solid when exiting pairing mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-763">如果配對成功，則控制器會震動一次，如果配對失敗和超時，則會震動三次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-763">The controller vibrates once if pairing was successful or vibrates three times if pairing is unsuccessful and times out.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-764">**控制器連接/中斷與電腦的連線**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-764">**Controller connects/disconnects from PC**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-765">當控制器開啟後，控制器會成功連線到電腦，而在使用時，控制器會與電腦中斷連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-765">The controller successfully connects to PC after you turn it on, or the controller disconnects from the PC during use for some reason.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-766">控制器會在電腦連線或中斷連接時震動一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-766">The controller vibrates once on PC connection or disconnection.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-767">**電力偏低等級**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-767">**Low Battery Level**</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-768">電池計量偏低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-768">The battery level is low.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-769">當電池計量偏低時，不會有 LED 或震動的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-769">There is no LED or vibration indication when battery is low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-770">耳機中控制器標記法的控制碼上有電池指標圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-770">There is a battery indicator icon on the handle of the controller representation in headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-771">當電池計量偏低時，指標圖示會顯示1/4 已滿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-771">When battery is low, the indicator icon will show 1/4 full.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-772">**電力不足等級**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-772">**Critical Battery Level**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba121-773">當電池計量為「重大」時開啟電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-773">During power on when battery level is "Critical".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-774">「重大」電池等級表示電源不足，控制器將會自動關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-774">"Critical" battery level means there is insufficient power and the controller will turn off automatically.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="ba121-775">當您開啟控制器時，控制器會震動三次，然後自動關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-775">The controller vibrates three times when you turn it on and then automatically turns off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-776">當您使用此狀態時，電池指示器圖示會顯示紅色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-776">As you approach this state, the battery indicator icon will display red.</span></span> |


### <a name="how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-777">如何得知我是否使用藍牙技術？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-777">How can I tell if I'm using Bluetooth technology?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-778">移動控制器使用許多消費者裝置中的相同藍牙技術，其設計目的是要與任何最近的電腦上所包含的藍牙功能搭配使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-778">Motion controllers use the same Bluetooth technology found in many consumer devices and are designed to work with the Bluetooth capability included in any recent PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-779">若要確認您的電腦具有藍牙無線電 (如果裝置通過混合現實相容性檢查程式，則應該) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-779">To verify that your PC has a Bluetooth radio (it should if the device passed the Mixed Reality Compatibility Checker):</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-780">以滑鼠右鍵按一下 Windows [開始] 功能表，然後選取 [裝置管理員]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-780">Right click on the Windows Start Menu and select "Device Manager".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-781">展開 [藍牙] 區段，並尋找介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-781">Expand the Bluetooth section and look for an adapter.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-782">如果您的電腦沒有藍牙，則建議使用的其中一個轉換器是 [PLUGABLE USB 藍牙4.0 低功耗微介面卡](https://www.amazon.com/Plugable-Bluetooth-Adapter-Raspberry-Compatible/dp/B009ZIILLI/ref=sr-1-1?ie=UTF8&qid=1490148230&sr=8-1&keywords=plugable+broadcom)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-782">If your PC doesn’t have Bluetooth, one recommended dongle is the [Plugable USB Bluetooth 4.0 Low Energy Micro Adapter](https://www.amazon.com/Plugable-Bluetooth-Adapter-Raspberry-Compatible/dp/B009ZIILLI/ref=sr-1-1?ie=UTF8&qid=1490148230&sr=8-1&keywords=plugable+broadcom).\</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-783">![範例裝置管理員的螢幕擷取畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-783">![Screenshot of an Example Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-784">介面卡是藍牙無線電。](images/devicemanagerbtadapterpic.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-784">The Adapter is the Bluetooth radio.](images/devicemanagerbtadapterpic.png)</span></span> 


### <a name="my-pc-has-bluetooth-technology-but-im-having-problems-with-my-motion-controllers"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-785">我的電腦具有藍牙技術，但我的動作控制器有問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-785">My PC has Bluetooth technology but I'm having problems with my motion controllers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-786">移動控制器應該與其他 Bluetooth 鍵盤、滑鼠和遊戲控制器搭配運作，但其體驗會依您使用的鍵盤、滑鼠或遊戲控制器的模型而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-786">Motion controllers should work with other Bluetooth keyboards, mice, and game controllers, but the experience will vary depending on the model of keyboard, mouse, or game controller you use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-787">以下是您可以用來改善效能的一些事項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-787">Here are some things you can do to improve performance:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-788">如果您的電腦具有藍牙，但仍有行動電話控制器的問題，請考慮將您的藍牙無線電取代為插入 USB 的 Plugable 外部藍牙介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-788">If your computer has Bluetooth but you are still having problems with the motion controllers, consider replacing your Bluetooth radio with the Plugable external Bluetooth Adapter plugged into USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-789">請注意，您一次只能有一個使用中的藍牙無線電配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-789">Note that you can only have one Bluetooth radio adapter active at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-790">如果您在現有的電臺以外插入外部電臺，您必須在裝置管理員中停用現有的藍牙無線電 (以滑鼠右鍵按一下介面卡，然後選取 [停用裝置] ) 並取消配對所有先前的藍牙裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-790">If you plug in an external radio in addition to an existing radio you need to disable your existing Bluetooth radio in Device Manager (right click on the adapter and select "Disable Device") and un-pair/re-pair all of your previous Bluetooth devices.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-791">如果您使用的是 USB Bluetooth 介面卡，請將它連接到 USB 2.0 埠 (2.0 埠為黑色，且未標示為 "SS" ) （如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-791">If you're using a USB Bluetooth Adapter, connect it to a USB 2.0 port (2.0 ports are black and aren’t labeled "SS"), if available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-792">埠應與下列實體分開：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-792">The port should be physically separated from:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="ba121-793">HMD USB 連接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-793">the HMD USB connector</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="ba121-794">快閃磁碟機</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-794">flash drives</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="ba121-795">硬碟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-795">hard drives</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="ba121-796">像是鍵盤/老鼠的無線 USB 接收器，理想的情況是將 USB Bluetooth 介面卡盡可能插入電腦的相反端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-796">wireless USB receivers like those for keyboards/mice Ideally, plug the USB Bluetooth Adapter into the opposite side of the computer as far as possible from these other connectors.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-797">請勿安裝任何協力廠商軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-797">Do not install any third party software.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-798">關閉 [藍牙設定] 視窗（如果已開啟）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-798">Close the Bluetooth settings window if it's open.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-799">讓它在背景中保持開啟，表示會對藍牙通訊協定進行許多額外的呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-799">Leaving it open in the background means that a lot of extra calls are made to the Bluetooth protocol.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-800">在 [藍牙 & 其他裝置] 下，停用 [顯示通知以使用迅速配對] 設定，以減少主機無線電掃描活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-800">Disable "Show notification to connect using Swift Pair" setting under Bluetooth & other devices to reduce host radio scanning activity.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-801">如果您使用的是內部藍牙卡，請確定您使用的是外部藍牙天線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-801">If you are using an internal Bluetooth card, please ensure you are using an external Bluetooth antenna.</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-802">在此情況下，缺乏外部藍牙天線的已知原因是追蹤問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-802">Lack of external Bluetooth antenna in this case is known to cause tracking issues.</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="ba121-803">如果無法運作，請在停用內部藍牙之後，使用外部藍牙轉換器 (USB) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-803">If this doesn’t work, please use an external Bluetooth dongle (USB) after disabling the internal Bluetooth.</span></span>
