* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-804">裝置必須出現在藍牙設定的 [滑鼠、鍵盤 & 畫筆] 類別之下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-804">It is important that the device appears under the "Mouse, Keyboard & Pen" category in the Bluetooth settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-805">如果在 [其他裝置] 下，則將並配對裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-805">If under "Other devices" then unpair and pair the device.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-806">移除、取消配對，以及關閉藍牙耳機和喇叭的電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-806">Remove, un-pair, and power off Bluetooth headphones and speakers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-807">Windows Mixed Reality 不支援這些。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-807">These are not supported with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-808">您可以在混合現實耳機上使用耳機插口或內建喇叭，以獲得最佳的音訊體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-808">You can use the headphone jack or built-in speakers on your Mixed Reality headset for the best audio experience.</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-pair-my-motion-controllers-to-a-windows-mixed-reality-headset-with-built-in-bluetooth-radio-or-return-them-to-their-factory-pairing"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-809">我要如何將動畫控制器與內建藍牙無線電的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機配對，或將它們退回給廠配對？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-809">How can I pair my motion controllers to a Windows Mixed Reality headset with built-in Bluetooth radio, or return them to their factory pairing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-810">某些 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機（包括 Acer OJO 500 和 Samsung 電影對白 +）有內建的藍牙無線電波可搭配運動控制器使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-810">Some Windows Mixed Reality headsets, including the Acer OJO 500 and Samsung Odyssey+, have built-in Bluetooth radios for use with motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-811">隨附于這些耳機的移動控制器會預先配對至原廠的耳機，不需要您的電腦具有個別的藍牙無線電。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-811">The motion controllers that come with these headsets are pre-paired to the headset from the factory, and do not require your PC to have a separate Bluetooth radio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-812">您 _可以_ 手動將這些移動控制器與電腦的藍牙無線電配對，例如與沒有內建藍牙無線電的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機搭配使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-812">These motion controllers _can_ be manually paired to your PC's Bluetooth radio, for example, for use with Windows Mixed Reality headsets that do not have built-in Bluetooth radios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-813">若要將移動控制器歸還給站配對，或將它們與內建藍牙無線電的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機配對，請執行耳機的裝置附屬應用程式 (例如，"Acer OJO 500" 應用程式或 "Samsung HMD 電影對白 + Setup" 應用程式，會在首次耳機插入) 時自動安裝，並遵循行動電話控制器配對的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-813">To return the motion controllers to their factory pairing, or to pair them with a Windows Mixed Reality headset with built-in Bluetooth radio, run the headset's device companion app (for example, the "Acer OJO 500" app or the "Samsung HMD Odyssey+ Setup" app, automatically installed the first time the headset is plugged in) and follow the instructions for motion controller pairing.</span></span>


## <a name="performance-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-814">效能問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-814">Performance questions</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-tell-if-the-windows-mixed-reality-headset-is-rendering-at-60hz-or-90hz-framerate"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-815">如何判斷 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機是否以60Hz 或90Hz 幀呈現？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-815">How can I tell if the Windows Mixed Reality headset is rendering at 60Hz or 90Hz framerate?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-816">檢查 **裝置入口網站 > 效能** ] 索引標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-816">Check the **Device Portal > Performance** tab.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-817">**注意** ：如果您的離散 GPU 具有 HDMI 2.0 埠，而 CPU 有四個以上的實體核心，則應該取得 90 Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-817">**Note** : If you have a discrete GPU with HDMI 2.0 ports and a CPU with four or more physical cores, you should be getting 90 Hz.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-818">如果您的 GPU 只有 HDMI 1.4 輸出，您可以使用 DisplayPort 至 [HDMI 2.0 介面卡](https://holodocswiki.com/wiki/Recommended_adapters_for_Windows_Mixed_Reality_Capable_PCs) 作為因應措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-818">If your GPU only has a HDMI 1.4 output, you can use a DisplayPort to [HDMI 2.0 adapter](https://holodocswiki.com/wiki/Recommended_adapters_for_Windows_Mixed_Reality_Capable_PCs) as a workaround.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-819">**注意** ： **耳機顯示器 > 視覺品質設定** 只會影響 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁體驗的呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-819">**Note** : The **Headset display > visual quality settings** only affect the rendering of the Windows Mixed Reality Home experience.</span></span>

### <a name="what-do-i-do-if-my-pc-appears-to-be-running-slowly"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-820">如果電腦的執行速度很慢，該怎麼辦？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-820">What do I do if my PC appears to be running slowly?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-821">系統可能會因為許多原因而變慢，在大部分情況下，這會在幾秒鐘後減少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-821">The system may be sluggish for many reasons and in most cases this will subside after a few seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-822">如果您在一段長時間內遇到此問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-822">If you experience this problem over long periods of time:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-823">關閉桌面上所有未使用的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-823">Close all unused application on the desktop.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-824">確定您的膝上型電腦已插入電源來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-824">Ensure that your laptop is plugged into a power source.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-825">確定電腦未準備好。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-825">Ensure that the PC is not warming up.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-826">降低 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁的視覺品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-826">Lower the visual quality in your Windows Mixed Reality Home.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-827">確定您的電腦有最新的圖形驅動程式 (請參閱) 的 [圖形驅動程式] 區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-827">Ensure that you have the latest graphics drivers for your PC (see the graphics drivers section).</span></span>

### <a name="my-pc-is-warming-up-as-i-run-the-mixed-reality-experiences-how-do-i-keep-it-cool"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-828">我的電腦在執行混合現實體驗時正在準備。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-828">My PC is warming up as I run the Mixed Reality experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-829">如何? 保持不酷？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-829">How do I keep it cool?</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-830">確定電池已收費，而且電源來源已插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-830">Ensure that the battery is charged and power source is plugged in.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-831">請確定不會封鎖進出電腦的風扇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-831">Make sure that the fans that blow air into or out of the PC are not blocked.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-832">在相當酷炫的環境中使用電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-832">Use the PC in a relatively cool environment.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-833">請確定沒有任何熱度來源 (例如，在電腦上) 的太陽或熱度通風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-833">Make sure there are no heat sources (for example, the sun or heat vents) pointed at the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-visuals-are-choppy-load-slowly-or-dont-look-good"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-834">我的視覺效果斷斷續續、載入速度很慢，或看起來沒問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-834">My visuals are choppy, load slowly, or don't look good.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-835">請確定您的耳機已插入您電腦上正確的圖形配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-835">Make sure your headset is plugged into the correct graphics card on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-836">有些電腦具有整合式和離散的圖形配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-836">Some PCs have both integrated and discrete graphics cards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-837">離散卡片通常會提供最佳效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-837">The discrete card will generally provide the best performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-838">[深入瞭解電腦硬體](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-838">[Learn more about PC hardware](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-839">關閉桌面上未使用的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-839">Close unused applications on your desktop.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-840">確定您的耳機適合 snugly (將它移到較低和更高或左右左右，以調整) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-840">Make sure your headset fits snugly (move it lower and higher or left and right to adjust).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-841">在 [ **設定] > 混合現實 > 耳機顯示** 中調整您的耳機視覺效果設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-841">Adjust your headset's visual settings in **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-842">當「視覺品質」設定為「自動」時，我們會為您的電腦選擇最佳的混合現實體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-842">When "Visual quality" is set to "Automatic", we'll choose the best mixed reality experience for your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-843">如需更多視覺效果詳細資料的體驗，請將「視覺品質」設定為「高」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-843">For an experience with more visual detail, set "Visual quality" to "High".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-844">如果您的視覺效果斷斷續續，您可能會想要選取較低的設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-844">If your visuals are choppy, you may want to select a lower setting.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-845">請嘗試調整耳機的校正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-845">Try adjusting your headset's calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-846">應調整鏡頭以符合您的 interpupillary 距離 (IPD) ，也就是瞳孔之間的距離。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-846">The lenses should be adjusted to match your interpupillary distance (IPD), the distance between your pupils.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-847">如果您不知道您的 IPD，optometrist 應該能夠為您進行測量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-847">If you don't know your IPD, an optometrist should be able to measure it for you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-848">也有設計來測量 IPD 的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-848">There are also websites designed to measure IPD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-849">知道您的 IPD 之後，請使用耳機的校正旋鈕來進行調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-849">Once you know your IPD, use your headset's calibration knob to make adjustments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-850">如果耳機沒有校正旋鈕，請選取 [ **設定] > 混合現實 > 耳機顯示** 並調整「校正控制項」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-850">If the headset doesn't have a calibration knob, select **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display** and adjust the "Calibration control".</span></span>


## <a name="tracking-system-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-851">追蹤系統問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-851">Tracking system problems</span></span>

### <a name="the-system-cannot-find-the-boundary-and-im-being-presented-with-setup-ui"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-852">系統找不到界限，而且我會看到安裝程式 UI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-852">The system cannot find the boundary and I'm being presented with setup UI.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-853">這表示追蹤系統無法辨識您的環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-853">This means that the tracking system was unable to recognize your environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-854">如果您是在新的環境中，您必須設定 [界限](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality#set-up-your-room-boundary)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-854">If you are in a new environment, you must set up the [boundary](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality#set-up-your-room-boundary).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-855">如果您先前曾在此環境中使用裝置，並設定界限：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-855">If you have previously used the device in this environment and set up a boundary:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-856">請確定房間有足夠的光線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-856">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-857">請確定您已將裝置磨損，並已查看房間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-857">Make sure you have worn the device and looked around the room.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-858">裝置必須觀察您的環境，以瞭解其所在位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-858">The device must observe your environment to know where it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-859">如果它位於桌上或桌上，它就不會找到您的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-859">It will not find your bounds if it is sitting on a desk or table.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-860">將裝置拔下，關閉 Windows Mixed Reality，然後重新插入裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-860">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug the device in again.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-861">您的環境中可能已有某些變更，而裝置無法再辨識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-861">Something may have changed in your environment and the device no longer recognizes it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-862">嘗試設定新的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-862">Try setting up a new boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-863">如果這些步驟無法解決問題，則請刪除您的環境資料，然後再次設定界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-863">If these steps do not resolve the problem, then delete your environment data and set up the boundary again.</span></span>

### <a name="the-system-is-presenting-me-with-ui-that-asks-me-to-choose-setup-for-all-experiences-or-seatedstanding-and-i-see-my-bounds"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-864">系統會向我呈現 UI，要求我針對所有體驗或站上/站選設定，並看到我的範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-864">The system is presenting me with UI that asks me to choose setup for all experiences or seated/standing, and I see my bounds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-865">裝置花太多時間找出界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-865">The device is taking too long to find the bounds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-866">您可以藉由選擇使用界限的選項來略過此訊息，系統會將您的界限帶到您的 Windows Mixed Reality Home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-866">You can bypass this message by choosing the option to use a boundary and you will be taken to your Windows Mixed Reality Home with your bounds present.</span></span>

### <a name="i-frequently-see-a-message-saying-ive-lost-my-bounds"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-867">我經常會看到一則訊息，指出「我已遺失界限」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-867">I frequently see a message saying "I've lost my bounds".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-868">追蹤系統正在追蹤及識別您的環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-868">The tracking system is having a hard time tracking and identifying your environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-869">在此狀態下，裝置不會再顯示您的界限，而耳機會切換至3DOF，讓您能夠上下加減一點到真實世界中的專案，直到它再次找到您的界限為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-869">In this state, the device can no longer display your bounds and the headset switches to 3DOF to keep you from to bumping into things in the real world until it locates your bounds again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-870">修正方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-870">To fix this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-871">請確定房間有足夠的光線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-871">Make sure that the room has enough light.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-872">如果您最近 redecorated 或改建年份空間，請重新執行安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-872">Rerun the setup if you recently redecorated or remodeled the room.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-873">拔掉裝置，關閉 Windows Mixed Reality，然後重新插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-873">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug it in again.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-874">清除您的環境資料，然後再次設定裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-874">Clear your environment data and set up the device again.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-875">如果訊息持續存在，請洽詢客戶支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-875">If the message persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="i-can-look-around-but-i-cant-translate-im-stuck-in-3dof"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-876">我可以查看，但無法轉譯 (我卡在 3DOF) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-876">I can look around but I can't translate (I'm stuck in 3DOF).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-877">這表示追蹤系統無法產生姿勢，或應用程式已停止使用新的姿勢資料來呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-877">This means that the tracking system cannot generate pose, or the application has stopped using new pose data to render.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-878">檢查下列項目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-878">Check the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-879">請確定房間有足夠的光線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-879">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-880">請確定房間有足夠的詳細資料可供追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-880">Make sure the room has enough details to track.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-881">拔下裝置，關閉 Windows Mixed Reality，然後重新插入裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-881">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug in the device again.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-882">如果訊息持續存在，請洽詢客戶支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-882">If the message persists, contact customer support</span></span>

### <a name="the-view-in-the-hmd-is-completely-frozen"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-883">HMD 中的視圖已完全凍結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-883">The view in the HMD is completely frozen.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-884">這通常表示應用程式或系統層級元件已失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-884">This usually means the application or a system level component has failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-885">嘗試：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-885">Try to:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-886">按 [首頁] 按鈕以離開應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-886">Press the "home" button to leave the application.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-887">拔掉裝置，關閉 [MRP]，然後重新插入裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-887">Unplug the device, close MRP and plug the device back in.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-888">重新開機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-888">Reboot the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="i-frequently-see-a-black-border-around-the-edges-of-the-view-in-the-hmd-sometimes-it-looks-like-im-looking-down-a-tunnel"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-889">我經常會在 HMD 的邊緣周圍看到黑色框線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-889">I frequently see a black border around the edges of the view in the HMD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-890">有時看起來像是一個通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-890">Sometimes it looks like I'm looking down a tunnel.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-891">這表示應用程式無法在您的電腦上叫用畫面播放速率，而且系統會使用舊的畫面格在 HMD 中呈現視圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-891">This means that the application is not able to hit frame rate on your PC and the system is using old frames to render the view in the HMD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-892">由於應用程式只會轉譯您正在查看的世界部分，如果它們不會一直碰到畫面播放速率，系統就會嘗試繼續從先前的觀點來呈現世界，並以黑色填滿遺漏的詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-892">Since applications only render the part of the world you are looking at, if they do not consistently hit their frame rates, then the system will attempt to continue to render the world from a previous point of view and will fill in the missing details with black.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-893">如果經常發生這種情況：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-893">If this happens frequently:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-894">關閉或終止所有不必要的程式，以釋放記憶體和 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-894">Close or terminate all unneeded programs to free up memory and CPU.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-895">減少應用程式中的詳細資料設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-895">Reduce detail settings in your application.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-896">減少 Windows Mixed Reality 設定中的詳細資料設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-896">Reduce detail settings in Windows Mixed Reality settings.</span></span>

### <a name="the-view-in-the-hmd-is-jittering-and-stuttering-a-lot"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-897">HMD 中的觀點是 jittering，而間斷情形很多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-897">The view in the HMD is jittering and stuttering a lot.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-898">有幾個原因可能會發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-898">There are several reasons this may happen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-899">主要的原因是系統無法轉譯內容到耳機，或追蹤系統發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-899">The primary causes are the system not being able to render content to the headset, or the tracking system is experiencing problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-900">檢查下列項目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-900">Check the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-901">確定您的電腦未遭受資源爭用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-901">Make sure your PC is not under resource contention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-902">開啟工作管理員並確保您的計算資源是免費的 (例如，80% 的 CPU 可用、ram 400MB 和磁片 IO 低於 80% ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-902">Open Task Manager and ensure your compute resources are free (for example, 80% CPU free, 400MB of ram and disk IO is below 80%).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-903">確定您擁有最新的硬體圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-903">Make sure you have the latest graphics drivers for your hardware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-904">如需詳細資訊，請參閱圖形驅動程式一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-904">See the graphics driver section for more info.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-905">請確定房間有足夠的光線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-905">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-906">將裝置拔下，關閉 Windows Mixed Reality，然後重新插入裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-906">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug the device in again.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-907">重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-907">Reboot your PC.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-908">如果問題持續發生，請洽詢客戶支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-908">If the problem persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-briefly-froze-and-perhaps-tilted-or-flipped-upside-before-returning-to-normal"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-909">在恢復正常之前，此世界短暫旁邊，可能是傾斜或翻轉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-909">The world briefly froze and perhaps tilted or flipped upside before returning to normal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-910">這可能是因為應用程式或系統層級元件發生嚴重錯誤，或是暫時性缺乏記憶體或 CPU 資源所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-910">This could be caused by an app or system level component hitting a fatal error, or a temporary lack of memory or CPU resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-911">檢查下列項目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-911">Check the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-912">開啟 [工作管理員]，並確定您有至少20% 的 CPU 可用和400MB 記憶體可用 (例如 80% CPU 可用、ram 400MB 和磁片 IO 低於 80% ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-912">Open "Task Manager" and ensure you have at least 20% CPU free and 400MB memory free (e.g. 80% CPU free, 400MB of ram and disk IO is below 80%).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-913">開啟 [事件檢視器]，然後移至 [ **Windows 記錄檔] > [應用程式** ]，並在凍結時移至 [錯誤事件] 專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-913">Open "Event Viewer" and go to **Windows Logs > Application and Error** event entries around the time of the freeze.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-914">查看是否有任何進程損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-914">Check to see if any processes crashed.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-915">如果此問題持續發生，請嘗試重新開機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-915">Try rebooting the PC if this problem persists.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-flipped-upside-down-momentarily-and-returned-to-normal"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-916">世界會短暫反轉，並返回正常狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-916">The world flipped upside down momentarily and returned to normal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-917">這通常是因為從耳機取得感應器資料以通知追蹤演算法的錯誤所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-917">This is typically caused by errors in obtaining sensor data from the headset to inform the tracking algorithms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-918">如果經常發生這種情況：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-918">If this happens frequently:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-919">將耳機插入不同的 USB 3.0 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-919">Plug the headset into a different USB 3.0 port.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-920">將耳機直接插入電腦，而不是 USB 3.0 中樞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-920">Plug the headset directly into the PC rather than a USB 3.0 hub.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-921">如果問題持續發生，請洽詢客戶支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-921">If the problem persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-is-tilted-but-i-can-navigate-and-walk-around-fine-in-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-922">世界是傾斜的，但我可以在 Windows Mixed Reality 中流覽和四處解說。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-922">The world is tilted but I can navigate and walk around fine in Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-923">這通常是因為感應器資料錯誤會記錄到儲存在您電腦上的環境資料中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-923">This is usually caused by sensor data errors being recorded into the environment data that is stored on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-924">這可能會導致 Windows Mixed Reality 出現傾斜，有時會永久出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-924">This can cause the Windows Mixed Reality to appear tilted, sometimes permanently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-925">嘗試下列作業：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-925">Try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-926">拔掉 HMD，關閉 Windows Mixed Reality 並插上耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-926">Unplug the HMD, close Windows Mixed Reality and plug the headset back in.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-927">重新開機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-927">Reboot the PC.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-928">清除您的環境資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-928">Clear your environment data.</span></span>

## <a name="webvr-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-929">WebVR 問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-929">WebVR questions</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-see-my-controllers-when-viewing-vr-content-from-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-930">從 Edge 查看 VR 內容時，為什麼看不到我的控制器？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-930">Why can’t I see my controllers when viewing VR content from Edge?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-931">並非所有 WebVR 內容都是為了支援移動控制器而撰寫的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-931">Not all WebVR content is authored to support motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-932">WebVR 可讓內容開發人員支援不同類型的輸入，例如遊戲控制器或動作控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-932">WebVR allows developers of content to support different types of input, such as game controllers or motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-933">如果您在網站上看不到您的控制器，可能是沒有動作控制器支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-933">If you do not see your controllers on a site, it likely doesn’t have motion controller support.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-use-the-mouse-in-an-immersive-webvr-view"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-934">為什麼我無法在沉浸式 WebVR 視圖中使用滑鼠？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-934">Why can't I use the mouse in an immersive WebVR view?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-935">這是 WebVR 規格的選擇性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-935">This is an optional feature of the WebVR specification.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-936">並非所有瀏覽器都支援這項功能，而且並非所有 WebVR 內容都是為了支援滑鼠輸入而撰寫的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-936">Not all browsers support this feature, and not all WebVR content is authored to support mouse input.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-937">WebVR 可讓內容開發人員支援不同類型的輸入，例如滑鼠、鍵盤、遊戲控制器或移動控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-937">WebVR allows content developers to support different types of input, such as mouse, keyboard, game controllers or motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-938">滑鼠輸入行為會依瀏覽器而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-938">Mouse input behavior varies per browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-939">在 Microsoft Edge 中，網站作者必須確保在向耳機呈現時，會使用「pointerlock」來執行滑鼠輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-939">Within Microsoft Edge, website authors must ensure they take 'pointerlock' when presenting to the headset for mouse input to work.</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-my-controller-look-like-a-viveoculus-has-strange-orientation-or-the-buttons-are-incorrectly-mapped"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-940">為什麼我的控制器看起來像是 Vive/Oculus，有奇怪的方向，或按鈕的對應不正確？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-940">Why does my controller look like a Vive/Oculus, has strange orientation, or the buttons are incorrectly mapped?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-941">網站可能沒有完整的移動控制器支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-941">The website likely doesn’t have full motion controller support.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-view-360-degree-videos-from-youtubefacebookvimeothe-guardiannew-york-times-etc-from-edge-in-vr"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-942">為什麼我無法從 Youtube/Facebook/Vimeo/守護者/紐約時間，以及在 VR 的邊緣查看360度的影片？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-942">Why can’t I view 360 degree videos from Youtube/Facebook/Vimeo/The Guardian/New York Times, etc. from Edge in VR?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-943">就像任何其他 web 規格或標準一樣，作者也可以選擇執行它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-943">Just like any other web specification or standard, the author has the choice to implement it or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-944">有一種 WebVR 規格，可讓網站直接從瀏覽器啟動 VR 體驗，而這些網站的作者目前尚未執行此規格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-944">There is a WebVR specification that allows websites to launch VR experiences directly from the browser and the authors of these websites have not implemented this specification at this time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-945">某些平臺上可能會有可下載的應用程式，可讓您從這些廠商查看 VR 內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-945">There may be downloadable apps on some platforms that enable viewing of VR content from these vendors.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-enter-vr-from-firefox-or-chrome"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-946">為什麼我無法從 Firefox 或 Chrome 輸入 VR？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-946">Why can’t I enter VR from Firefox or Chrome?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-947">目前只有 Edge Windows Mixed Reality 裝置才支援 WebVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-947">WebVR is only supported by Windows Mixed Reality devices in Edge at this time.</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-enter-vr-from-a-website-why-do-i-see-a-blank-screen-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-948">當我從網站輸入 VR 時，為什麼我會在耳機中看到空白畫面？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-948">When I enter VR from a website, why do I see a blank screen in my headset?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-949">網站可能尚未支援多 GPU 機器 (包括混合式 GPU 膝上型電腦) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-949">The website may not have implemented support for Multi GPU machines (including Hybrid GPU laptops).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-950">嘗試：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-950">Try to:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-951">重新載入頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-951">Reload the page.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-952">在桌上型電腦上，將耳機插入與顯示 Microsoft Edge 的監視器相同的圖形介面卡中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-952">On desktop machines, plug the headset into the same graphics adapter as the monitor that is displaying Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-953">將兩者插入至較高的電源圖形配接器，而不是整合式圖形介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-953">Plug both into the higher powered graphics card, not into the integrated graphics adapter.</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-exit-vr-when-watching-a-video-from-edge-the-sound-continues-playing-but-the-edge-window-is-grayed-out"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-954">當我在從 Edge 觀看影片時結束 VR 時，音效會持續播放，但 Edge 視窗會呈現灰色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-954">When I exit VR when watching a video from Edge, the sound continues playing but the Edge window is grayed out.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-955">這是在混合現實 cliffhouse 中從邊緣執行 WebVR 時的已知問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-955">This is a known issue when running WebVR from Edge in the Mixed Reality cliffhouse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-956">若要解決此問題，請在鍵盤上按下 esc 鍵，而不是按下 [windows] 按鈕以結束 WebVR 體驗，或是選取它，然後停止影片來啟用灰色的邊緣視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-956">To resolve it, press escape on the keyboard rather than pressing the windows button to exit the WebVR experience, or activate the greyed out Edge window by selecting it and then stop the video.</span></span>

### <a name="can-i-use-webvr-on-the-hololens"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-957">我可以在 HoloLens 上使用 WebVR 嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-957">Can I use WebVR on the HoloLens?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-958">Microsoft 目前尚未在 HoloLens 上宣佈任何關於 WebVR 的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-958">Microsoft has not announced anything about WebVR on the HoloLens at this point.</span></span>

### <a name="why-is-my-view-at-floor-level-when-viewing-webvr-content-from-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-959">當您從 Edge 觀看 WebVR 內容時，為什麼我的視圖位於樓層層？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-959">Why is my view at floor level when viewing WebVR content from Edge?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-960">網站未適當支援 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-960">The website does not properly support Windows Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-961">若要解決這個問題︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-961">To work around this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-962">將耳機放在您的空間地板上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-962">Place the headset on the floor of your space.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-963">使用桌面上的 Microsoft Edge 流覽至 [WebVR] 頁面， (不在混合現實) 內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-963">Navigate to the WebVR page using Microsoft Edge on your desktop (not within Mixed Reality).</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-964">按一下網頁上的按鈕，以輸入 VR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-964">Click the button on the webpage to Enter VR.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-965">等候5-10 秒，讓體驗完全進入沉浸式模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-965">Wait 5-10 seconds for the experience to fully enter immersive mode.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-966">拿到耳機，把它放在您的頭部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-966">Pick up the headset and place it on your head.</span></span>

### <a name="the-display-is-very-low-resolution-in-some-webvr-experiences"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-967">在某些 WebVR 體驗中，顯示器的解析度極低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-967">The display is very low resolution in some WebVR experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-968">網站未適當支援高解析度耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-968">The websites do not properly support high resolution headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-969">若要解決此問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-969">To workaround this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-970">如果從 (桌面啟動 WebVR，而不是從 Mixed Reality cliffhouse) 內，請確定視窗在進入 VR 之前都已最大化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-970">If launching WebVR from the desktop (as opposed to from within the Mixed Reality cliffhouse), ensure the window is maximized prior to Entering VR.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-971">請避免在您輸入 VR 之後調整 Microsoft Edge 視窗的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-971">Avoid resizing the Microsoft Edge window after you have entered VR.</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-the-webvr-immersive-view-exit-when-i-change-browser-tabs"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-972">為什麼在變更瀏覽器索引標籤時，WebVR 沉浸式視圖結束？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-972">Why does the WebVR immersive view exit when I change browser tabs?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-973">這是預期行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-973">This is expected behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-974">基於安全性理由，只有作用中的瀏覽器索引標籤可以存取 connected 耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-974">For security reasons, only the active browser tab can access connected headsets.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-hear-audio-on-a-particular-webvr-experience"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-975">為什麼我無法聆聽特定 WebVR 體驗的音訊？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-975">Why can't I hear audio on a particular WebVR experience?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-976">網站可能使用 OGG 音訊檔案格式，Microsoft Edge 目前不支援此格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-976">The website may be using the OGG audio file format, which Microsoft Edge does not currently support.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-977">您可以直接向 [問題追蹤](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-edge/platform/issues/)程式中的 Microsoft Edge 瀏覽器小組報告已中斷的網站，或使用 [#EdgeBug](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2016/08/11/edgebug-twitter/)主題標籤，透過 twitter 來回報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-977">You can report broken sites directly to the Microsoft Edge browser team in the [issue tracker](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-edge/platform/issues/), or via twitter using [#EdgeBug hashtag](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2016/08/11/edgebug-twitter/).</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-haptic-feedback-not-work-in-webvr-with-motion-controllers"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-978">為什麼 Haptic 意見反應無法在使用移動控制器的 WebVR 中運作？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-978">Why does Haptic feedback not work in WebVR with motion controllers?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-979">Microsoft Edge 目前不支援 WebVR 遊戲台 API 擴充功能上的 haptics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-979">Microsoft Edge does not currently support haptics on the WebVR gamepad API extensions.</span></span>


## <a name="steamvr-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-980">SteamVR 問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-980">SteamVR questions</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-play-steamvr-games-in-my-windows-mixed-reality-immersive-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-981">我要如何在 Windows Mixed Reality 的沉浸式耳機播放 SteamVR 遊戲？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-981">How can I play SteamVR games in my Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-982">您必須在電腦上安裝 SteamVR Windows Mixed Reality，並設定 SteamVR：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-982">You must install Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR on your PC and set up SteamVR:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-983">[下載並安裝 SteamVR](https://steamcdn-a.akamaihd.net/client/installer/SteamWindowsMRInstaller.exe)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-983">[Download and install SteamVR](https://steamcdn-a.akamaihd.net/client/installer/SteamWindowsMRInstaller.exe).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-984">開始 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-984">Start SteamVR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-985">SteamVR 教學課程應該會自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-985">The SteamVR Tutorial should start automatically.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-986">將您的耳機連接到您的電腦，然後開啟您的動作控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-986">Connect your headset to your PC and turn on your motion controllers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-987">一旦載入 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁，並顯示您的控制器，請在您的桌面上開啟串流應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-987">Once the Windows Mixed Reality home has loaded and your controllers are visible, open the Steam app on your desktop.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-988">使用流應用程式從您的串流庫啟動 SteamVR 遊戲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-988">Use the Steam app to launch a SteamVR game from your Steam library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-989">若要在不離開耳機的情況下啟動 SteamVR 遊戲，您可以在 Windows Mixed Reality **開始 > 所有應用程式** 中找到並啟動遊戲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-989">To launch SteamVR games without taking off your headset, you can find and launch them under Windows Mixed Reality's **Start > All Apps** .</span></span> 

### <a name="i-get-a-message-that-says-to-use-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality-you-need-to-install-the-latest-windows-update-or-windows-developer-mode-required"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-990">我收到一則訊息，指出「若要搭配 Windows Mixed Reality 使用 SteamVR，您必須安裝最新的 Windows Update」或「需要 Windows 開發人員模式」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-990">I get a message that says “To use SteamVR with Windows Mixed Reality, you need to install the latest Windows Update" or "Windows Developer Mode Required".</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-991">確定您的電腦正在執行最新版本的 Windows 10。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-991">Make sure your PC is running the latest version of Windows 10.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-992">若要檢查這一點，請移至 [ **設定] > 系統 > 相關資訊** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-992">To check this, go to **Settings  > System > About** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-993">在 [Windows 規格] 下，確定 [作業系統組建] 為16299.64 或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-993">Under "Windows specifications", make sure "OS Build" is 16299.64 or greater.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-994">請確定您沒有任何更新正在等候下載或安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-994">Make sure you don’t have any updates waiting to download or install.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-995">移至 [ **設定] > 更新 & 安全性 > Windows Update** 然後選取 [檢查更新]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-995">Go to **Settings  > Update & Security > Windows Update** and select "Check for updates".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-996">您可能必須多次檢查更新，因此請繼續檢查更新，直到沒有其他可用的更新，然後重新開機電腦為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-996">You may have to check for updates multiple times so keep checking for updates until no further updates are available and then restart your PC.</span></span>

### <a name="steamvr-is-crashing-after-updating-windows"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-997">SteamVR 在更新 Windows 之後損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-997">SteamVR is crashing after updating Windows.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-998">某些較舊版本的 SteamVR Windows Mixed Reality 不再與 Windows 相容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-998">Some older versions of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR are no longer compatible with Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-999">您可能會有 SteamVR 的舊版 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-999">You may have an old version of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1000">確定您是最新的：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1000">To ensure that you are up to date:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1001">在您的串流媒體櫃中，移至 [ **軟體 >] Windows Mixed Reality 以進行 SteamVR** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1001">In your Steam library, go to **Software > Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR** .</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1002">以滑鼠右鍵按一下該檔案，然後移至 [屬性]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1002">Right click it and go to "Properties".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1003">選取 [更新] 索引標籤，然後選取 [永遠將此應用程式保持在最新狀態]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1003">Select the "Update" tab and select "Always keep this application up to date".</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1004">請前往 [本機檔案] 索引標籤，然後選取 [驗證應用程式檔的完整性]，來強制更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1004">Force the update by going to the "Local Files" tab and selecting “Verify integrity of application files”.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1005">重新開機流和 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1005">Restart Steam and SteamVR.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1006">如果 SteamVR 在更新之後仍損毀，您可能會在電腦上有兩個用於 SteamVR 的 Windows Mixed Reality 安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1006">If SteamVR is still crashing after updating you may have two installations of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR on your machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1007">若要確認是否為這種情況：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1007">To confirm if this is the case:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1008">找出%localappdata%\openvr\openvrpaths.vrpath，然後在 [記事本] 中開啟它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1008">Locate %localappdata%\openvr\openvrpaths.vrpath and open it in Notepad.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1009">在 [外部驅動程式] 區段中，尋找 "MixedRealityVRDriver" 的多個專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1009">Under the "external drivers" sections look for multiple entries for "MixedRealityVRDriver"</span></span> 
   ```json
   "external_drivers" : [
      "D:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver",
      "E:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver"
   ],
   ```
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1010">如果您看到多個專案，請移除兩個專案中的舊專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1010">If you see multiple entries, remove the older of the two entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1011">請注意，當您只有一個專案時，行尾應該不會再有逗號，例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1011">Note that once you have only one entry there should no longer be a comma at the end of the line, for example:</span></span>
   ```json
   "external_drivers" : [
      "D:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver"
   ],
   ```
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1012">儲存並關閉檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1012">Save the file and close it.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1013">重新開機流和 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1013">Restart Steam and SteamVR.</span></span>

### <a name="my-controllers-arent-working-as-expected-in-steamvr"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1014">我的控制器在 SteamVR 中未如預期般運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1014">My controllers aren't working as expected in SteamVR.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1015">關閉 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1015">Close SteamVR.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1016">返回 Mixed Reality 首頁，並確認您的控制器如預期般運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1016">Return to the Mixed Reality Home and confirm that your controllers are working as expected.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1017">再次啟動 SteamVR 體驗，您的控制器應該恢復正常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1017">Launch the SteamVR experience again and your controllers should be back to normal.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1018">如果問題持續發生，請使用混合現實類別下的 [Windows 意見反應中樞](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4021566/windows-10-send-feedback-to-microsoft-with-feedback-hub-app) 提出意見反應，並在摘要中包含 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1018">If issues persist please file feedback using the [Windows Feedback Hub](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4021566/windows-10-send-feedback-to-microsoft-with-feedback-hub-app) under the Mixed Reality category and include SteamVR in the summary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1019">請注意，您將在不同的遊戲中使用不同的移動控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1019">Note that you'll use your motion controllers differently in different games.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1020">以下是一些可協助您開始使用的基本概念：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1020">Here are a few basics to help you get started:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1021">若要開啟 [串流] 儀表板，請在左側操縱杆上按直向下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1021">To open the Steam dashboard, press straight down on the left thumbstick.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1022">若要結束 SteamVR 遊戲並回到 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁，請按 [Windows] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1022">To exit a SteamVR game and return to the Windows Mixed Reality home, press the Windows button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1023">然後選取畫面上顯示的 Mixed Reality 首頁按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1023">Then select the Mixed Reality Home button that appears on screen.</span></span>

### <a name="my-left-and-right-controllers-are-reversed-in-steamvr"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1024">我的左側和右側控制器會在 SteamVR 中反轉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1024">My left and right controllers are reversed in SteamVR.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1025">從您的控制器開始遊戲，然後開啟左側的遊戲，再按右邊一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1025">Start the game with your controllers off and then turn the left one on, followed by the right one.</span></span>

### <a name="my-games-are-running-slowly"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1026">我的遊戲執行速度很慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1026">My games are running slowly.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1027">確認您的電腦符合 Windows Mixed Reality 的 SteamVR 規格</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1027">Confirm that your PC meets the specifications for SteamVR in Windows Mixed Reality</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1028">確認您的電腦符合您所播放 SteamVR 遊戲的規格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1028">Confirm that your PC meets the specifications for the SteamVR game you are playing.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1029">在桌面上的混合實境入口中，選取 [暫停] 以停止桌面預覽版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1029">In Mixed Reality Portal on your desktop, select "Pause" to stop desktop preview.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1030">遵循上面的指示，確定您正在執行 Windows 10 組建16299.64 或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1030">Follow the instructions above to make sure you are running Windows 10 build 16299.64 or later.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1031">請確定您的電腦具有最新的圖形驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1031">Make sure your PC has the latest graphics drivers.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1032">檢查工作管理員，查看您的電腦上有哪些其他處理常式正在執行，並耗用資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1032">Check Task Manager to see what other processes might be running on your PC and consuming resources.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1033">查看串流是否正在背景下載遊戲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1033">Check to see if Steam is downloading a game in the background.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1034">這可能會耗用資源，讓遊戲的執行效能不佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1034">This can consume resources and make games run poorly.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1035">已知的效能問題會影響沒有可見視窗的小型應用程式類別，例如 SteamVR Home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1035">There is a known performance issue that affects a small class of apps that do not have a visible window, for example, SteamVR Home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1036">大部分的應用程式並不屬於這個類別，未來的更新將會提供修正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1036">The vast majority of apps do not fall into this category, and a fix will be available in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1037">如果您仍在遇到未預期的效能問題，請使用 Windows 意見反應中樞傳送意見反應給我們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1037">If you're still running into unexpected performance issues, please send us feedback using the Windows Feedback Hub.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1038">請務必遵循指示來 [納入 SteamVR 效能追蹤](using-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality.md#sharing-feedback-on-steamvr)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1038">Make sure to follow the instructions to [include a SteamVR Performance Trace](using-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality.md#sharing-feedback-on-steamvr).</span></span> 

### <a name="steamvr-is-showing-a-compositor-error-for-example-shared-ipc-compositor-connect-failed-400"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1039">SteamVR 顯示組合器錯誤 (例如「共用的 IPC 組合器連接失敗 (400) 」 ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1039">SteamVR is showing a compositor error (for example, "Shared IPC Compositor Connect Failed (400)").</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1040">已知的問題是，如果您的耳機和主要監視器位在兩個不同的視訊卡上，就會發生這種情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1040">There is a known issue where this can happen if your headset and primary monitor are on two different video adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1041">將您的監視器附加至與耳機相同的介面卡，並將該監視設定為 [設定] 應用程式中的主要監視 **> 系統 > 顯示** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1041">Attach your monitor to the same adapter as your headset and configure that monitor to be the primary monitor in **Settings app > System > Display** .</span></span>

### <a name="steamvr-content-appears-in-the-wrong-place-like-beneath-the-floor-or-above-my-head"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1042">SteamVR 內容會顯示在錯誤的位置，例如在地面下方或上方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1042">SteamVR content appears in the wrong place, like beneath the floor or above my head.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1043">重設您的位置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1043">Reset your position:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1044">按一下左邊控制器的操縱杆以顯示「SteamVR 儀表板」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1044">Click the left controller's thumbstick to bring up the "SteamVR Dashboard".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1045">選取 [設定] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1045">Select the "Settings" button.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1046">選取 [重設已安裝的位置]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1046">Select "Reset Seated Position".</span></span>

### <a name="my-steam-app-closed-unexpectedly"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1047">我的流應用程式意外關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1047">My Steam app closed unexpectedly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1048">如果您鎖定電腦畫面、移除耳機、切換使用者，或電腦進入睡眠狀態，則會關閉流應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1048">The Steam app will close if you lock your PC screen, remove your headset, switch users, or if your PC goes to sleep.</span></span>


## <a name="speech-and-audio-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1049">語音和音訊問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1049">Speech and audio problems</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-hear-any-sound-in-my-headset-or-sound-is-playing-through-my-computer-instead-of-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1050">我無法聽到耳機中的任何聲音，或是透過電腦而非耳機播放音效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1050">I can't hear any sound in my headset, or sound is playing through my computer instead of my headset.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1051">如果您的沉浸式耳機未包含內建耳機，您必須將耳機連接到耳機上的音訊插孔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1051">If your immersive headset doesn’t include built-in headphones, you’ll need to connect headphones to the audio jack on the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1052">插座通常位於耳機面板或鏡頭的後方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1052">The jack is often located just behind or under the headset visor or lenses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1053">如果找不到，請洽詢您的耳機製造商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1053">Check with your headset manufacturer if you can't find it.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1054">有些音訊耳機具有可控制音量的實體按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1054">Some audio headsets have physical buttons to control the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1055">如果音訊無法運作，請檢查磁片區是否已關閉或靜音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1055">If audio isn't working, check to see whether the volume is turned down or muted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1056">Windows Mixed Reality 是設計用來在執行混合實境入口時，透過沉浸式耳機播放音效，而您也有連接耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1056">Windows Mixed Reality is designed to play sound through your immersive headset when the Mixed Reality Portal is running and you have headphones connected to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1057">當您將耳機移開或翻轉面板時，請關閉混合實境入口的應用程式，或當該應用程式未使用15分鐘時，音訊會切換至您的預設 Windows 播放裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1057">When you take the headset off or flip the visor up, close the Mixed Reality Portal application, or when that app has not been used for 15 minutes, audio will switch to your default Windows playback device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1058">您可以在 [ **設定 > 混合現實 > 音訊和語音** ] 中變更此設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1058">You can change this setting in **Settings > Mixed reality > Audio and speech.**</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1059">請確定您的音訊耳機已完全插入音訊插孔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1059">Make sure your audio headset is plugged into the audio jack completely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1060">尤其是 Acer 耳機可能需要更多的護理，以確保音訊耳機都已插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1060">The Acer headset in particular may require more care to ensure the audio headset is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1061">檢查音訊耳機/麥克風是否已插入耳機，而不是電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1061">Check that the audio headset/microphone is plugged into the headset and not the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1062">Windows 音效主控台只會顯示已啟用的音訊端點，而不會顯示已停用的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1062">The Windows Sound Control Panel only shows enabled audio endpoints, not disabled endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1063">當您未戴耳機時，耳機音訊裝置將會停用，因此您必須以滑鼠右鍵按一下音效控制台，然後選擇 [顯示已停用的裝置] 以查看它;裝置名稱為「Realtek USB 2.0 音訊」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1063">The headset audio device will be disabled when you're not wearing the headset, so you have to right-click in the sound control panel and choose "Show disabled devices" to see it; the device name is "Realtek USB2.0 Audio".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1064">這麼做之後，您可以將 [屬性] 頁面中的名稱變更為您可以更輕鬆辨識的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1064">Once you do this, you can change the name in the "Properties" page to something you'll recognize more easily.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1065">您可以針對 [播放] 和 [錄製] 索引標籤進行這項作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1065">You can do this for both the playback and recording tabs.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1066">如果您的音訊無法在混合現實應用程式中運作 (例如，Netflix) ，這可能是因為已知的問題，Windows Mixed Reality 不會自動更新以符合作業系統版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1066">If your audio is not working in Mixed Reality apps (for example, Netflix), this may be caused by a known issue where Windows Mixed Reality is not be automatically updated to match the OS version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1067">若要修正此問題並獲得最佳的混合現實體驗，請移至 [ **設定] > 更新 & 安全性 > Windows Update > 檢查更新** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1067">To fix this issue and get the best Mixed Reality experience, go to **Settings > Update & Security > Windows Update > Check for Updates** .</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1068">**注意：** Windows Mixed Reality 空間音訊最適合搭配內建或直接連線到您的沉浸式耳機的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1068">**Note:** Windows Mixed Reality spatial audio works best with headphones built into or connected directly to your immersive headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1069">連接到電腦的電腦喇叭或耳機可能無法正常適用于空間音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1069">PC speakers or headphones connected to the PC might not work well for spatial audio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1070">**注意：** Windows Mixed Reality 不支援藍牙音訊耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1070">**Note:** Windows Mixed Reality doesn’t support Bluetooth audio headsets.</span></span>

### <a name="im-experiencing-sudden-volume-changes-lost-audio-or-buzzing"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1071">我遇到突然的音量變更、音訊遺失或蜂鳴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1071">I'm experiencing sudden volume changes, lost audio, or buzzing.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1072">某些應用程式（包括透過 SteamVR 啟動的許多應用程式）可能會在音訊裝置隨您啟動或停止混合實境入口時，遺失音訊或停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1072">Some applications, including many of those launched through SteamVR, can lose audio or hang when the audio device changes as you start or stop the Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1073">開啟混合實境入口應用程式之後，請重新開機應用程式以修正此錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1073">Restart the app after you have opened the Mixed Reality Portal app to correct this.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1074">如果另一個多媒體 USB 裝置 (例如網路凸輪) 與 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機共用相同的內部或外部 USB 集線器，則耳機的音訊插孔/耳機可能偶爾會有噪音音效或音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1074">If another multimedia USB device (such as a web cam) shares the same internal or external USB hub with the Windows Mixed Reality headset, the headset's audio jack/headphones may occasionally have a buzzing sound or no audio at all.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1075">將您的耳機插入使用不同中樞或中斷連接/停用其他 USB 多媒體裝置的 USB 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1075">Plug your headset into a USB port that uses a different hub or disconnect/disable your other USB multimedia device.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1076">如果您注意到耳機有大量的雜訊，則電腦的 USB 集線器可能無法提供足夠的電源給 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1076">If you notice a loud burst of noise from headphones connected to the headset, it is possible that the PC's USB hub is not able to provide enough power to the Windows Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1077">如果發生這種情況，請立即提出 [意見反應中樞](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-feedback) 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1077">If this occurs, file a [Feedback Hub](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-feedback) bug immediately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1078">因應措施包括不使用延伸模組纜線、使用專用的外部驅動 USB 3.0 中樞，或嘗試在電腦上使用不同的 USB 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1078">Workarounds that may help include not using extension cables, using a dedicated, external powered USB 3.0 HUB, or trying a different USB port on the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-bluetooth-audio-headset-isnt-working-as-expected"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1079">我的藍牙音訊耳機未如預期般運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1079">My Bluetooth audio headset isn't working as expected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1080">Microsoft 不建議搭配 Windows Mixed Reality 使用藍牙音訊耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1080">Microsoft does not recommend using Bluetooth audio headsets with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1081">藍牙音訊週邊設備無法正常搭配 Windows Mixed Reality 的語音和空間音效體驗，而且藍牙音訊耳機無法同時支援麥克風輸入和身歷聲輸出，因此當您將音訊或 hrtf 音效用於 gamechat 或其他語音輸入時，就不會聽到它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1081">Bluetooth audio peripherals do not work well with Windows Mixed Reality voice and spatial sound experiences, and Bluetooth audio headsets cannot support microphone input and stereo output at the same time, so you won't hear stereo or spatialized sound when using it for gamechat or other voice input.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1082">藍牙音訊耳機也會對您的移動控制器體驗產生負面影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1082">Bluetooth audio headsets can also negatively affect your motion controller experience.</span></span> 

### <a name="sound-isnt-coming-from-expected-directions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1083">音效並非來自預期的方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1083">Sound isn't coming from expected directions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1084">Windows Mixed Reality home 包含空間音效 (音訊，就像是來自家用) 的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1084">The Windows Mixed Reality home includes spatial sound (audio that sounds like it comes from the apps located in your home).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1085">當您在每個應用程式之間來回移動和移動時，音效方向和層級將會變得更進一步瞭解其真實性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1085">As you turn around and move closer or farther from each app, the sound direction and level will change to further the sense of realism.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1086">以下是非預期的音效方向的一些原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1086">Here are some reasons for unexpected sound directions:</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1087">當您從支援背景的音樂應用程式開啟並播放音樂時 (例如您家中的 Groove 音樂) ，然後開啟沉浸式的 VR 體驗 (例如遊戲) ，音樂應用程式的音效將 crossfade 從空間音效到身歷聲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1087">When you open and play music from a background-capable music app (like Groove Music) in your home and then open an immersive VR experience (like a game), the sound from the music app will crossfade from spatial sound to stereo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1088">它可能會比之前更大，因為您與音效之間已沒有任何距離。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1088">It may appear louder than before because there is no longer any distance between you and the sound.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1089">如果您在使用 Windows Mixed Reality 耳機之前，已在主機電腦上啟用 Cortana，您可能會遺失 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁中的應用程式所套用的空間音效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1089">If you had Cortana enabled on your host PC prior to using your Windows Mixed Reality headset, you may lose the spatial sound applied to the apps in your Windows Mixed Reality home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1090">若要修正此問題，請在啟動 Windows Mixed Reality 之前，關閉桌上型電腦應用程式視窗中的 [讓 Cortana 回應嗨 Cortana **>** ]，或從 Windows Mixed Reality home 中的桌面應用程式視窗中啟用 [耳機用 Windows Sonic]：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1090">To fix this, either turn off "Let Cortana respond to Hey Cortana" in **Settings > Cortana** on your desktop before launching Windows Mixed Reality, or enable "Windows Sonic for Headphones" from within the Desktop app window in Windows Mixed Reality home:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1091">以滑鼠左鍵按一下桌面工作列上的喇叭圖示，然後從音訊裝置清單中選取它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1091">Left-click the speaker icon on the desktop taskbar and select it from the list of audio devices.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1092">以滑鼠右鍵按一下桌面工作列上的喇叭圖示，然後在 [喇叭設定] 功能表中選取 [耳機用 Windows Sonic]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1092">Right-click the speaker icon on the desktop taskbar and select "Windows Sonic for Headphones" in the "Speaker setup" menu.</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1093">針對 (端點) 的所有音訊裝置重複這些步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1093">Repeat these steps for all of your audio devices (endpoints).</span></span>

### <a name="speech-commands-are-not-working-as-expected"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1094">語音命令未如預期般運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1094">Speech commands are not working as expected.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1095">若要使用語音命令，您電腦上的語音和語言設定必須設定為 [Windows Mixed Reality 中支援的語言](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039262/windows-10-mixed-reality-setup-faq#Languages)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1095">To use speech commands, speech and language settings on your PC must be set to a [language supported in Windows Mixed Reality](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039262/windows-10-mixed-reality-setup-faq#Languages).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1096">若要檢查您的 Windows 語音和語言設定，請選取 [ **設定 > 時間] & 語言 > 區域 & 語言** 和 **設定 > & 語言 > 語音** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1096">To check your Windows speech and language settings, select **Settings  > Time & language > Region & language** and **Settings  > Time & language > Speech** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1097">如果您的耳機沒有內建的麥克風，您將需要使用麥克風連接耳機或您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1097">If your headset doesn’t have a built-in microphone, you’ll need to attach headphones with a microphone to the headset or to your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1098">當您磨損麥克風時，若要讓麥克風自動切換至您的耳機，請移至 [ **設定] > Mixed reality > 音訊和語音** ，然後開啟 [當我磨損耳機時，切換到耳機 mic]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1098">To have microphone input switch automatically to your headset when you wear it, go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Audio and speech** , and turn on "When I wear my headset, switch to headset mic".</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1099">有些音訊耳機具有實體按鈕，可將麥克風靜音和取消靜音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1099">Some audio headsets have a physical button to mute and unmute the microphone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1100">如果語音命令無法運作，請查看您的麥克風是否已靜音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1100">If speech commands aren't working, check to see whether your microphone is muted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1101">使用麥克風 dangles 自 earbud 纜線的音訊耳機，在環境雜訊的環境中無法正常執行語音命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1101">Audio headsets with a microphone that dangles from the earbud cable do not perform well for voice commands in environments with ambient noise.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1102">當您第一次在混合實境入口會話中叫用 Cortana 時，Cortana 可能會變慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1102">Cortana can be slow the first time she is invoked in a Mixed Reality Portal session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1103">移至 **cortana 的 [設定] > cortana > 與 cortana** 通訊，並確定已啟用 [讓 Cortana 回應嗨 Cortana]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1103">Go to **Settings > Cortana > Talk to Cortana** and make sure "Let Cortana respond to Hey Cortana" is enabled.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1104">在某些電腦上，您耳機連接的麥克風的預設語音捕捉增益可能設定過低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1104">On some PCs, the default voice capture gain for your headset-connected microphone may be set too low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1105">如果您遇到不可靠的語音命令或聽寫，可以試著執行麥克風設定疑難排解員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1105">If you experience unreliable speech commands or dictation, you can try running the Microphone Setup troubleshooter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1106">您可以透過 [ **設定 > 時間] & 語言 > 語音** ，然後選取 [麥克風] 區段中的 [開始]，以連線到此疑難排解員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1106">You can reach this troubleshooter through the **Settings > Time & Language > Speech** , then select "Get Started" in the "Microphone" section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1107">您可以透過 Windows Mixed Reality 首頁中的桌面應用程式來執行這項操作，同時戴耳機以影響您用於 Windows Mixed Reality 的麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1107">Do this through the Desktop app in the Windows Mixed Reality home while wearing the headset to affect the microphone you use for Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1108">在疑難排解員 wizard 中選取適當的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1108">Select the appropriate endpoint in the troubleshooter wizard.</span></span>

### <a name="i-only-have-one-audio-headset-and-i-want-to-use-it-for-both-desktop-and-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1109">我只有一個音訊耳機，我想要將它用於桌上型電腦和我的耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1109">I only have one audio headset and I want to use it for both Desktop and my headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1110">如果您只有一個音訊耳機，而且沒有內建耳機的耳機，請將音訊耳機連接到主機電腦，而不是耳機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1110">If you only have one audio headset and do not have a headset with built in headphones, connect the audio headset to the host PC instead of the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1111">然後，在 [MRP 設定] 中關閉 [切換到耳機音訊]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1111">Then turn off "switch to headset audio" in the MRP settings.</span></span>

### <a name="i-want-to-switch-to-dolby-atmos-for-headphones"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1112">我想切換至 Dolby Atmos for Headphones。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1112">I want to switch to Dolby Atmos for Headphones.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1113">Windows Mixed Reality 環境和其應用程式使用耳機用 Windows Sonic 的空間音訊技術，其會針對混合現實體驗進行自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1113">Windows Mixed Reality environments and its applications use Windows Sonic for Headphones spatial audio technology which is customized for mixed reality experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1114">其他的空間音訊技術（例如 Dolby Atmos for Headphones）可以套用至全螢幕應用程式（例如 SteamVR 遊戲），但不適用於 Windows Mixed Reality shell 環境和應用程式 (例如，將網頁瀏覽器放在懸崖之屋的牆上，或使用) 空間音效和聲場設計的天空 Loft 耳機用 Windows Sonic。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1114">Other spatial audio technologies, like Dolby Atmos for Headphones, can be applied for full screen applications like SteamVR games but not for the Windows Mixed Reality shell environments and applications (such as placing a web browser on the wall of the Cliff House or the Sky Loft) which have been designed using Windows Sonic for Headphones spatial sound and acoustics.</span></span>


## <a name="questions-about-desktop-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1115">混合式桌上型電腦的相關問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1115">Questions about Desktop in Mixed Reality</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-access-my-pc-desktop-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1116">如何? 在混合的生活中存取我的電腦桌面？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1116">How do I access my PC desktop in Mixed Reality?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1117">您可以使用桌面應用程式，在混合現實中存取您的電腦桌面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1117">You can access your PC desktop in Mixed Reality using the Desktop app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1118">從 Windows 按鈕的耳機中啟動它 **> 所有應用程式 > 桌面** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1118">Launch it in the headset from **Windows Button > All apps > Desktop** .</span></span> 

### <a name="how-can-i-see-multiple-monitors-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1119">如何查看混合現實中的多個監視器？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1119">How can I see multiple monitors in Mixed Reality?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1120">根據預設，桌面應用程式會自動切換為顯示具有焦點的監視器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1120">By default, Desktop app automatically switches to display the monitor with focus.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1121">如果您想要在混合現實中看到所有的監視器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1121">If you want to see all of your monitors in Mixed Reality:</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1122">按一下應用程式左上角的 [監視] 圖示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1122">Click the monitor icon on the top left corner of the app</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1123">停用 [自動切換監視器]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1123">Disable "Automatically Switch Monitor"</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1124">挑選您想要查看的監視</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1124">Pick the monitor you want to see</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1125">啟動桌面應用程式的另一個實例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1125">Launch another instance of the Desktop app</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1126">選擇您想要在該實例上看到的監視器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1126">Pick the monitor you want to see on that instance</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1127">針對所有的實體監視器重複一次，請注意，每次您重新開機 Mixed Reality 時，都必須重新選擇要在每一個傳統型應用程式上顯示的監視器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1127">Repeat for all of your physical monitors Note that you will have to reselect the monitor to show on each Desktop app every time you restart Mixed Reality.</span></span> 

### <a name="my-desktop-app-only-shows-a-black-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1128">我的桌面應用程式只會顯示黑色畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1128">My Desktop app only shows a black screen.</span></span>
