<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1129">如果您的電腦有 Nvidia 混合式 GPU，問題可能是因為 Nvidia 裝置在離散 GPU （而非整合模式）上執行 runtimebroker.exe 所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1129">If your PC has an Nvidia hybrid GPU, the issue may be caused by Nvidia device running the runtimebroker.exe on the discrete GPU instead of the integrated one.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1130">若要修正此問題，請遵循「[如何? 建立新程式的 Optimus 設定](http://nvidia.custhelp.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/2615/~/how-do-i-customize-optimus-profiles-and-settings%3F)」底下的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1130">To fix this issue, follow these instructions under "[How do I create Optimus settings for a new program?](http://nvidia.custhelp.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/2615/~/how-do-i-customize-optimus-profiles-and-settings%3F)"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1131">新增 C:\windows\system32\runtimebroker.exe 並強制它在「整合式圖形」處理器上執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1131">to add C:\windows\system32\runtimebroker.exe and force it to run on the "Integrated graphics" processor.</span></span> 


## <a name="other-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1132">其他問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1132">Other Questions</span></span>

### <a name="my-samsung-odyssey-or-odyssey-headset-firmware-update-is-getting-stuck"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1133">我的 Samsung 電影對白或電影對白 + 耳機固件更新正在停滯中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1133">My Samsung Odyssey or Odyssey+ headset firmware update is getting stuck.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1134">Samsung 擁有併發布透過其 "Samsung HMD 電影對白 Setup" 和 "Samsung HMD 電影對白 + Setup" 裝置附屬應用程式所提供的耳機固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1134">Samsung owns and publishes headset firmware updates delivered via their "Samsung HMD Odyssey Setup" and "Samsung HMD Odyssey+ Setup" Device Companion apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1135">如需有關 Samsung 固件更新問題的詳細資訊和協助，請與 Samsung 客戶服務聯繫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1135">For more details and for help with Samsung firmware update issues, please reach out to Samsung Customer Service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1136">如果固件更新程式停滯，而且沒有超過五分鐘的進度：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1136">If the firmware update process is getting stuck, and there has been no progress for more than five minutes:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1137">暫時拔掉所有其他 USB 裝置，然後重試一次固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1137">Unplug all of your other USB devices temporarily and retry the firmware update.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1138">將 Samsung 耳機連接到您電腦上的其他 USB 3.0 埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1138">Connect your Samsung headset to a different USB 3.0 port on your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1139">停用和/或卸載任何可能幹擾固件更新的軟體，例如 Gb 的 AORUS App Center。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1139">Disabling and/or uninstall any software installed that may interfere with firmware updates, like Gigabyte's AORUS App Center.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1140">使用不同的電腦來執行 Samsung 耳機固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1140">Use a different PC to perform the Samsung headset firmware update.</span></span>

### <a name="my-wi-fi-slows-down-when-im-using-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1141">當我使用 Windows Mixed Reality 時，我的 Wi-fi 會變慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1141">My Wi-Fi slows down when I'm using Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1142">如果您使用 2.4 GHz Wi-fi 連線，則您的移動控制器可能會減緩 Wi-fi。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1142">If you're using a 2.4GHz Wi-Fi connection, your motion controllers might slow down your Wi-Fi.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1143">請嘗試下列其中一項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1143">Try one of the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1144">切換至5GHz 的 Wi-fi 連線（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1144">Switch to a 5GHz Wi-Fi connection, if one is available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1145">[深入了解](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4000461)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1145">[Learn more](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4000461).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1146">使用個別的 Bluetooth 介面卡，將您的動作控制器連接到您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1146">Use a separate Bluetooth adapter to connect your motion controllers to your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1147">請參閱 [建議的介面卡](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1147">See [recommended adapters](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines).</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-message-that-said-to-plug-in-and-charge-my-pc-why"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1148">我收到一則訊息，表示插入和收取電腦的費用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1148">I got a message that said to plug in and charge my PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1149">為何會這樣？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1149">Why?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1150">如果您使用的是膝上型電腦，則在電腦同時完全收取和插入電源時，Windows Mixed Reality 的效果最佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1150">If you're using a laptop, Windows Mixed Reality works best when the PC is both fully charged and plugged in.</span></span> 

### <a name="what-is-the-experience-options-setting"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1151">何謂體驗選項設定？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1151">What is the Experience options setting?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1152">體驗選項設定 ( **設定 > 混合現實 > 耳機顯示 > 體驗選項** ) 可讓您變更 Windows Mixed Reality 效能設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1152">The Experience options setting ( **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display > Experience options** ) allows you to change the Windows Mixed Reality performance settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1153">這可讓您在各種內容中選擇硬體設定的最佳可能體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1153">This enables you to choose the best possible experience for your hardware configuration across a range of content.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1154">所有系統都可使用90Hz 體驗，但您可能會想要嘗試自動查看您偏好的設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1154">The 90Hz experience is available to all systems, but you might want to try Automatic to see which setting you prefer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1155">選項如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1155">Here are the options:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1156">自動： Windows Mixed Reality 將決定硬體設定的最佳體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1156">Automatic: Windows Mixed Reality will determine the best experience for your hardware configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1157">對於大部分的人來說，這是開始使用的最佳選擇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1157">For most people, this is the best choice to start with.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1158">60Hz：將重新整理頻率設定為60Hz，並關閉特定功能，例如混合實境入口中的影片捕獲和預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1158">60Hz: Sets the refresh rate to 60Hz and turns off certain features, such as video capture and preview in Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1159">90Hz：將更新頻率設定為90Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1159">90Hz: Sets the refresh rate to 90Hz.</span></span>

### <a name="what-languages-are-supported-in-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1160">Windows Mixed Reality 支援哪些語言？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1160">What languages are supported in Windows Mixed Reality?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1161">Windows Mixed Reality 提供下列語言版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1161">Windows Mixed Reality is available in the following languages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1162">如果您的電腦設定為不同的語言，您仍然可以使用 Windows Mixed Reality，但介面會以英文 (顯示) ，而且語音命令和聽寫將無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1162">If your PC is set to a different language, you can still use Windows Mixed Reality, but the interface will appear in English (United States), and speech commands and dictation won't be available.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1163">簡體中文 (中國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1163">Chinese Simplified (China)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1164">英文 (澳大利亞)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1164">English (Australia)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1165">英文 (加拿大)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1165">English (Canada)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1166">英文 (英國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1166">English (Great Britain)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1167">英文 (美國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1167">English (United States)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1168">法文 (加拿大)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1168">French (Canada)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1169">法文 (法國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1169">French (France)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1170">德文 (德國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1170">German (Germany)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1171">義大利文 (義大利)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1171">Italian (Italy)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1172">日文 (日本)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1172">Japanese (Japan)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1173">西班牙文 (墨西哥)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1173">Spanish (Mexico)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1174">西班牙文 (西班牙)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1174">Spanish (Spain)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1175">Windows Mixed Reality 螢幕小鍵盤僅限英文 (美國) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1175">The Windows Mixed Reality onscreen keyboard is English (United States) only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1176">若要以另一種語言輸入文字，請使用連接到您電腦的實體鍵盤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1176">To enter text in another language, use a physical keyboard connected to your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1177">您也可以使用上面所列的其中一種支援 Windows Mixed Reality 語言的聽寫，只要在螢幕小鍵盤上選取 [麥克風] 即可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1177">You can also use dictation in one of the supported Windows Mixed Reality languages listed above—just select microphone on the onscreen keyboard.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1178">Windows Mixed Reality 也提供下列語言版本，不需要語音命令或聽寫功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1178">Windows Mixed Reality is also available in the following languages without speech commands or dictation features:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1179">繁體中文 (臺灣和香港特別行政區) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1179">Chinese Traditional (Taiwan and Hong Kong)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1180">荷蘭文 (荷蘭)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1180">Dutch (Netherlands)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1181">韓文 (韓國)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1181">Korean (Korea)</span></span>

### <a name="i-have-questions-about-my-headset-hardware"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1183">我有關于耳機硬體的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1183">I have questions about my headset hardware.</span></span>

## <a name="how-to-uninstall-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1186">如何卸載 Windows Mixed Reality</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1186">How to uninstall Windows Mixed Reality</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-uninstall-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1187">如何? 卸載 Windows Mixed Reality？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1187">How do I uninstall Windows Mixed Reality?</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1188">中斷耳機與電腦的連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1188">Disconnect your headset from your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1189">關閉混合實境入口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1189">Close Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1190">移至 [  **開始] > 設定 > 混合現實** ，然後選取 [卸載]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1190">Go to  **Start > Settings > Mixed Reality** and select "Uninstall".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1191">當您準備好再次使用耳機時，請將其插入，混合實境入口將會帶您完成設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1191">When you're ready to start using your headset again, plug it in, and Mixed Reality Portal will take you through setup.</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-we-couldnt-finish-uninstalling-windows-mixed-reality-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1192">我收到「我們無法完成卸載 Windows Mixed Reality」訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1192">I got a "We couldn't finish uninstalling Windows Mixed Reality" message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1193">這表示某些檔案（包括您的環境相關資訊）仍可能在您的電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1193">This means that some files, including information about your environment, might still be on your computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1194">如果您決定稍後重新安裝 Windows Mixed Reality，這可能會造成問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1194">This can cause problems if you decide to reinstall Windows Mixed Reality later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1195">您可以藉由修改登錄和使用 Windows PowerShell 來執行命令，以手動方式從電腦移除任何剩餘的 Windows Mixed Reality 資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1195">You can manually remove any remaining Windows Mixed Reality info from your PC by modifying the registry and using Windows PowerShell to run commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1196">_如果您不正確地修改登錄，可能會發生嚴重的問題。請務必小心遵循這些步驟。若要新增保護，請先備份登錄再進行修改，以便在問題就會發生時進行還原。_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1196">_If you modify the registry incorrectly, serious problems might occur. Make sure to follow these steps carefully. For added protection, back up your registry before you modify it so you can restore it if a problem occurrs._</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1197">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [如何在 Windows 中備份和 restory 登錄](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/322756/how-to-back-up-and-restore-the-registry-in-windows)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1197">For more info, see [How to back up and restory the registry in Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/322756/how-to-back-up-and-restore-the-registry-in-windows).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1198">若要使用下列命令卸載 Windows mixed reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1198">To uninstall Windows mixed reality using these commands:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1199">重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1199">Restart your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1200">在 **搜尋** 方塊中，輸入 "regedit"，然後選取 **[是]** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1200">In the **Search** box, type "regedit" and then select **Yes** .</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1201">移除下列登錄值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1201">Remove the following registry values:</span></span>
   <ul>
    <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1202"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic</b>，然後刪除 <b>FirstRunSucceeded</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1202"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>FirstRunSucceeded</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1203"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic\speechandaudio</b>，然後刪除 <b>PreferDesktopSpeaker</b> 和 <b>PreferDesktopMic</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1203"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic\SpeechAndAudio</b>, then delete <b>PreferDesktopSpeaker</b> and <b>PreferDesktopMic</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1204"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\ Speech_OneCore &gt; Settings\Holographic</b>，然後刪除 <b>DisableSpeechInput</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1204"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Speech_OneCore&gt; Settings\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>DisableSpeechInput</b>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1205">注意：您必須針對已使用 Windows Mixed Reality 之電腦上的每個使用者帳戶，刪除 HHKEY_CURRENT_USER 中的登錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1205">Note:the registry items in HHKEY_CURRENT_USER must be deleted for every user account on the PC that has used Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1206"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\perceptionsimulationextensions</b>，然後刪除 <b>DeviceID</b> 和 <b>模式</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1206"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\PerceptionSimulationExtensions</b>, then delete <b>DeviceID</b> and <b>Mode</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1207"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic</b>，然後刪除 <b>OnDeviceLearningCompleted</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1207"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>OnDeviceLearningCompleted</b>.</span></span></li> 
   </ul><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1208">
4. 移除下列登錄機碼：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1208">
4. Remove the following registry keys:</span></span> <ul>
   <li> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1209"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\HoloSI</b></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1209"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\HoloSI</b></span></span></li> 
   <li> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1210"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE \Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\HoloSI</b></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1210"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\HoloSI</b></span></span></li> 
   <li> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1211"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\ Speech_OneCore \Settings\HolographicPreferences</b></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1211"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Speech_OneCore\Settings\HolographicPreferences</b></span></span></li><br/></ul><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1212">
5. 關閉登錄編輯程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1212">
5. Close the Registry Editor.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1213">6. 流覽至 **C:\Users\user name\appdata\local\packages\ Microsoft.Windows.HolographicFirstRun_cw5n1h2txyewy \localstate** ，然後刪除 **RoomBounds.js** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1213">6. Navigate to **C:\Users\user name\AppData\Local\Packages\Microsoft.Windows.HolographicFirstRun_cw5n1h2txyewy\LocalState** , and then delete **RoomBounds.json** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1214">針對已使用 Windows Mixed Reality 的每個使用者重複此步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1214">Repeat this for each user who has used Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1215">7. 開啟系統管理員命令提示字元並流覽至 **C:\ProgramData\WindowsHolographicDevices\SpatialStore\HoloLensSensors** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1215">7. Open admin cmd prompt and navigate to **C:\ProgramData\WindowsHolographicDevices\SpatialStore\HoloLensSensors** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1216">然後刪除 **HeadTracking data** 資料夾的內容 (但不) 資料夾本身。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1216">Then delete the contents of the **HeadTracking data** folder (but not the folder itself).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1217">8. 在 **搜尋** 方塊中輸入 "powershell"，以滑鼠右鍵按一下 [ **Windows PowerShell** ]，然後選取 [以 **系統管理員身分執行** ]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1217">8. Type "powershell" in the **Search box** , right-click **Windows PowerShell** , and then select **Run as administrator** .</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba121-1218">9. 在 Windows PowerShell 中，執行下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1218">9. In Windows PowerShell, do the following:</span></span> <ul>
   <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1219">在命令提示字元中複製並貼上下列命令，然後按 Enter： <b>Dism/Online/Get-Capabilities</b></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1219">Copy and paste the following at the command prompt, then press Enter: <b>Dism /online /Get-Capabilities</b></span></span></li> 
   <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1220">複製以類比.. (開頭的功能身分識別，如果&#39;t，則表示此專案不&#39;安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1220">Copy the Capability Identity that begins with Analog.Holographic.Desktop (if it isn&#39;t there, that means this item isn&#39;t installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba121-1221">在此情況下，請跳至步驟 10 ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1221">In that case, skip to step 10 ).</span></span></li> 
   <li><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1222">複製並貼上下列命令提示字元，然後按 Enter： <b>Dism/Online/Remove-Capability/CapabilityName：在最後一個步驟中複製的功能身分識別</b></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1222">Copy and paste the following command prompt, then press Enter: <b>Dism /online /Remove-Capability /CapabilityName:the Capability Identity copied in the last step</b></span></span></li>
   </ul><span data-ttu-id="ba121-1223">
10. 重新開機您的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba121-1223">
10. Restart your PC.</span></span>
